﻿                                                   Preamble                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
This Contract is entered into in Beijing on this 8th day of September, 1997, by and between                     <br /><br /><br />
China National Petroleum Corporation (hereinafter abbreviated as “CNPC”), a company organized                   <br /><br /><br />
and existing under the laws of the People's Republic of China, having its headquarters domiciled in             <br /><br /><br />
Beijing, the People’s Republic of China as one part; and the following company:                                 <br /><br /><br />
Pan-China Resources Ltd., a company organized and existing under the laws of the British                        <br /><br /><br />
Virgin Islands, having its headquarters domiciled in Calgary, Canada; (hereinafter referred to as the           <br /><br /><br />
“Foreign Contractor”) as the other part.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                 WITNESSETH                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, all Petroleum resources under the territory, internal waters, territorial sea, and                     <br /><br /><br />
continental shelf of the People's Republic of China and within the limits of national jurisdiction of the       <br /><br /><br />
People's Republic of China are owned by the People's Republic of China;                                         <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, CNPC shall be responsible for business matters in respect of the exploitation of                       <br /><br /><br />
land Petroleum resources in cooperation with foreign enterprises, and for negotiating, entering into            <br /><br /><br />
and implementing Contracts for the exploitation of land Petroleum resources in cooperation with                 <br /><br /><br />
foreign enterprises and to have the exclusive right to explore for, develop and produce the Petroleum           <br /><br /><br />
in cooperation with foreign enterprises in areas approved by the State Council with the “Regulations            <br /><br /><br />
of the People's Republic of China Concerning the Exploitation of Onshore Petroleum Resources in                 <br /><br /><br />
Cooperation with Foreign Enterprises” (hereafter referred to as the “Petroleum Regulations”),                   <br /><br /><br />
promulgated by the State Council of the People's Republic of China on Oct. 7,1993;                              <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, CNPC has performed exploration work and has had a potential commercial                                 <br /><br /><br />
discovery in the Contract Areas; and                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, the Foreign Contractor desires and agrees to provide funds, and apply its                              <br /><br /><br />
appropriate and advanced technology and managerial experience to cooperate with CNPC for the                    <br /><br /><br />
exploitation of Petroleum resources within the Contract Area and agrees to be subject to the laws,              <br /><br /><br />
decrees, and other rules and regulations of the People’s Republic of China in the implementation of             <br /><br /><br />
the Contract.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 NOW, THEREFORE, IT IS MUTUALLY AGREED as hereafter set forth:                                                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                      Article 1                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                   Definitions                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
The following words and terms used in the Contract shall have, unless otherwise specified                   <br /><br /><br />
herein, the following meanings:                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
1.1    “Petroleum” means Crude Oil and Natural Gas deposited in the subsurface and being                    <br /><br /><br />
extracted or already extracted, including any valuable non-hydrocarbon substances produced in               <br /><br /><br />
association with Crude Oil and/or Natural Gas separated or extracted therefrom.                             <br /><br /><br />
1.2    “Crude Oil” means solid and liquid hydrocarbons in their natural state, including any                <br /><br /><br />
liquid hydrocarbons extracted from Natural Gas but excluding liquefied methane (CH4).                       <br /><br /><br />
1.3    “Natural Gas” means Non-associated Natural Gas and Associated Natural Gas in their                   <br /><br /><br />
natural state.                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.4    “Associated Natural Gas” means all gaseous hydrocarbons produced in association                      <br /><br /><br />
with Crude Oil from oil reservoirs, including residue gas remaining after the extraction of liquid          <br /><br /><br />
hydrocarbons therefrom.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
1.5    “Oil Field” means an accumulation of Petroleum within the Contract Area composed                     <br /><br /><br />
of one or several overlapping oil-bearing zones, within one trap or within associated traps of the same     <br /><br /><br />
independent geological structure, which may or may not be complicated by faulting, and which has            <br /><br /><br />
been determined to be of commercial value.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
1.6    “Petroleum Operations” means the Pilot Test Operations, the Development                              <br /><br /><br />
Operations, the Production Operations, and other activities related to these Operations carried out         <br /><br /><br />
under the Contract.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
1.7    “Pilot Test Operations” means study and operations conducted for the purpose of                      <br /><br /><br />
determining the economical efficiency for the reservoir(s) or payzone(s) within the Contract Area and       <br /><br /><br />
production activities conducted within the Pilot Test Area, including drilling, side tracking,              <br /><br /><br />
recompletion, stimulation and injectivity test, well group pilot displacement test and evaluations on       <br /><br /><br />
development geology of the reservoirs) or payzone(s) and reservoir engineering within the Contract          <br /><br /><br />
Area.                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
1.8    “Development Operations” means operations carried out for the realization of                         <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum production from the date of approval of the Overall Development Program for the Oil Field         <br /><br /><br />
by the Department or Unit, including design, construction, installation, drilling, and the related          <br /><br /><br />
research work as well as production activities carried out before the Date of Commencement of               <br /><br /><br />
Commercial Production.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.9    “Production Operations” means operations and all activities related thereto carried out              <br /><br /><br />
for Petroleum production of the Oil Field in the Contract Area from the Date of Commencement of             <br /><br /><br />
Commercial Production, such as extraction, injection, stimulation, treatment, storage, transportation,      <br /><br /><br />
lifting, etc.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
﻿1.10    “Contract Area” means a surface area demarcated with geographic coordinates for the             <br /><br /><br />
cooperative exploitation of Petroleum resources, and in the Contract, means the surface area stipulated <br /><br /><br />
in Article 3.1 hereof.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
1.11    “Pilot Test Area” means the surface area within the Contract Area where Pilot Test              <br /><br /><br />
Operations are conducted in accordance with Article 3.2 hereof.                                         <br /><br /><br />
1.12    “Development Area” means a portion of the Contract Area covering the Oil Field                  <br /><br /><br />
which has been designated for development, and delineated as such in the Overall Development            <br /><br /><br />
Program approved by the Department or Unit. The Development Area shall automatically cease to be        <br /><br /><br />
in force as of the date of approval of the Production Area by CNPC.                                     <br /><br /><br />
1.13    “Production Area” means a surface area within the Development Area for the purpose              <br /><br /><br />
of the performance of the Production Operations within the said Development Area after completion       <br /><br /><br />
of the Development Operations. The Production Area proposed by the Operator, demarcated by JMC          <br /><br /><br />
shall be submitted to CNPC for approval before the Date of Commencement of Commercial                   <br /><br /><br />
Production.                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
1.14    “Date of Commencement of Commercial Production” means the date of                               <br /><br /><br />
commencement of the production period for Crude Oil and/or Natural Gas from the Oil Field               <br /><br /><br />
announced by JMC in accordance with the provisions of Article 7.2.6 hereof after the completion of      <br /><br /><br />
the Development Operations as provided for in the approved Overall Development Program for the          <br /><br /><br />
said Oil Field, and after approval by CNPC.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
1.15    “Calendar Year” means a period of twelve (12) consecutive Gregorian months under                <br /><br /><br />
the Gregorian Calendar, beginning on the first day of January and ending on the thirty-first day of     <br /><br /><br />
December in the same year.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.16    “Contract Year” means a period of twelve (12) consecutive Gregorian months under                <br /><br /><br />
the Gregorian Calendar, within the term of the Contract, beginning on the Date of Commencement of       <br /><br /><br />
the Implementation of the Contract or any anniversary thereof.                                          <br /><br /><br />
1.17    “Production Year” means in respect of the Oil Field, a period of twelve (12)                    <br /><br /><br />
consecutive Gregorian months under the Gregorian Calendar, beginning on the Date of                     <br /><br /><br />
Commencement of Commercial Production of such Oil Field or any anniversary thereof.                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
1.18    “Calendar Quarter” means a period of three (3) consecutive Gregorian months under               <br /><br /><br />
the Gregorian Calendar, beginning on the first day of January, the first day of April, the first day of <br /><br /><br />
July, or the first day of October.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.19    “Development Well” means a well drilled after the date of approval of the Overall               <br /><br /><br />
Development Program for the Oil Field for the purpose of producing Petroleum, increasing                <br /><br /><br />
production or accelerating extraction of Petroleum, including production wells, injection wells and     <br /><br /><br />
dry holes.                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
1.20 “Work Program” means all types of plans formulated for the performance of the                      <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations, including plans for development and production.                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
1.21 “Overall Development Program” means a plan prepared by the Contractor for the                      <br /><br /><br />
development of the Oil Field which has been reviewed and adopted by JMC, confirmed by CNPC and          <br /><br /><br />
approved by the Department or Unit, and such plan shall include, but shall not be limited to,           <br /><br /><br />
﻿recoverable reserves, the Development Well pattern, master design, production profile, economic                               <br /><br /><br />
analysis and time schedule of the Development Operations.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
1.22    “LIBOR” means the seven-day term London Inter-Bank Offered Rate for U.S.                                              <br /><br /><br />
Dollars for similar amounts to the sums in question, quoted by Midland Bank in London at 11:00 a.m.                           <br /><br /><br />
on the first business day of the relevant period.                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
1.23    “Pilot Test Costs” means the expenses incurred for the completion of the Pilot Test                                   <br /><br /><br />
Operations and the activities related to the Pilot Test Operations, including the evaluations on the                          <br /><br /><br />
detailed development geology of the reservoirs) or payzone(s) and the reservoir engineering within                            <br /><br /><br />
the Contract Area, and the expenses incurred for preparation and application for approval of the                              <br /><br /><br />
Overall Development Program.                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
1.24    “Development Costs” means the expenses incurred for the design, construction and                                      <br /><br /><br />
installation of the equipment and facilities within the Contract Area and drilling of the development                         <br /><br /><br />
wells, as well as the Operating Costs incurred before the Date of Commencement of Commercial                                  <br /><br /><br />
Production after the approval of the Overall Development Program by the Department or Unit.                                   <br /><br /><br />
1.25    “Operating Costs” means the expenses incurred for the petroleum production from                                       <br /><br /><br />
the Date of Commencement of the Commercial Production, such as the expenses incurred for                                      <br /><br /><br />
extraction, injection, stimulation, disposal, storage, transportation and lifting, etc.                                       <br /><br /><br />
1.26    “Oil Field Straddling a Boundary” means the Oil Field extending from the Contract                                     <br /><br /><br />
Area to one or more other contract areas and/or areas in respect of which no Petroleum contracts have                         <br /><br /><br />
been signed.                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
1.27    “Annual Gross Production of Natural Gas” means the total amount of Natural Gas                                        <br /><br /><br />
produced from the Oil Field within the Contract Area considered separately in each Calendar Year,                             <br /><br /><br />
less the amount of Natural Gas used for Petroleum Operations and the amount of losses, which is                               <br /><br /><br />
saved and measured by a measuring device at the Delivery Point as specified in Article 14.2.1 hereof.                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.28 “Annual Gross Production of Crude Oil” means the total amount of Crude Oil                                               <br /><br /><br />
produced from the Oil Field within the Contract Area considered separately in each Calendar Year,                             <br /><br /><br />
less the amount of Crude Oil used for Petroleum Operations and the amount of losses, which is saved                           <br /><br /><br />
and measured by a measuring device at the Delivery Point as specified in Article 14.2.1 hereof.                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.29    “Contractor” means the Foreign Contractor specified in the Preamble hereto,                                           <br /><br /><br />
including assignee(s) in accordance with Article 23 hereof.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
1.30    “Parties” means CNPC and the Contractor.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.31    “Party” means either of the Parties.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                              1.32    “Operator” means the entity responsible for the performance of the Petroleum            <br /><br /><br />
Operations under the Contract.                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                              1.33    “Subcontractor” means an entity, which provides the Operator with goods or services     <br /><br /><br />
 the purpose of the Contract.                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                              1 *34 “Third Party” means any individual or entity except CNPC, the Contractor and any of       <br /><br /><br />
fteir Affiliates.                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                            7                                                 <br /><br /><br />
﻿1.35    “Chinese Personnel” means any citizen of the People's Republic of China, including          <br /><br /><br />
CNPC personnel and Chinese citizens employed by the Contractor and/or the Subcontractors),          <br /><br /><br />
involved in Petroleum Operations under the Contract.                                                <br /><br /><br />
1.36    “Expatriate Employee” means any person employed by the Contractor,                          <br /><br /><br />
Subcontractor(s), or CNPC who is not a citizen of the People's Republic of China. Overseas Chinese  <br /><br /><br />
who reside abroad and have the nationality of the People's Republic of China and other Chinese      <br /><br /><br />
abroad, when they are employed by the Contractor, Subcontractor(s) or CNPC, shall also be deemed    <br /><br /><br />
to be Expatriate Employees within the scope of the Contract.                                        <br /><br /><br />
1.37    “Affiliate” means in respect of the Contractor:                                             <br /><br /><br />
(a)    any entity in which any company comprising the Contractor directly or indirectly             <br /><br /><br />
holds fifty percent (50%) or more of the voting rights carried by its share capital; or             <br /><br /><br />
(b)    any entity which directly or indirectly holds fifty percent (50%) or more of the             <br /><br /><br />
aforesaid voting rights of any company comprising the Contractor; or                                <br /><br /><br />
(c)    any other entity whose aforesaid voting rights are held by an entity mentioned in (b)        <br /><br /><br />
above in an amount of fifty percent (50%) or more;                                                  <br /><br /><br />
“Affiliate” means, in respect of CNPC, any subsidiary, branch, or regional corporation of           <br /><br /><br />
CNPC and any entity in which CNPC directly or indirectly holds fifty percent (50%) or more of the   <br /><br /><br />
voting rights carried by its share capital.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
1.38    “Delivery Point” means a point or points agreed upon by the Parties for the delivery        <br /><br /><br />
of Petroleum located within or outside the Contract Area and specified in the Overall Development   <br /><br /><br />
Program.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
1.39    “Department or Unit” means the department or unit, which is authorized by the State         <br /><br /><br />
Council of the People's Republic of China to be responsible for administration of the Petroleum     <br /><br /><br />
industry of the People's Republic of China.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
1.40    “Date of Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract” means the first day            <br /><br /><br />
of the month following the month in which the Contractor has received the notification from CNPC of <br /><br /><br />
the approval of the Contract by the Ministry of Foreign Trade and Economic Cooperation of the       <br /><br /><br />
People's Republic of China.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                        Article 2                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                            Objective of the Contract                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
2.1    The objective of the Contract is to develop and produce Petroleum with proved                       <br /><br /><br />
commercial value in the Contract Area.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
2.2    The Contractor shall apply its appropriate and advanced technology and assign its                   <br /><br /><br />
competent experts to perform the Petroleum Operations.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
2.3    During the performance of the Petroleum Operations, the Contractor shall transfer its               <br /><br /><br />
technology to the Chinese Personnel and train them in accordance with Article 16 hereof and Annex          <br /><br /><br />
IV- Training of Chinese Personnel and Transfer of Technology.                                              <br /><br /><br />
2.4    The Contractor shall bear all the costs required for the Pilot Test Operations. If the              <br /><br /><br />
Contractor opts to enter into the development period, the Contractor shall bear all the costs required     <br /><br /><br />
for the Development Operations.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
2.5    The Petroleum produced from the Oil Field within the Contract Area shall, from the                  <br /><br /><br />
Date of Commencement of the Commercial Production, be allocated in accordance with Articles 13,            <br /><br /><br />
and/or 18 hereof.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
2.6    Nothing contained in the Contract shall be deemed to confer any right on the                        <br /><br /><br />
Contractor other than those rights expressly granted hereunder.                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                       Article 3                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                  Contract Area                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
3.1    The Contract Area as of the date of signature of the Contract, includes Zi Lai Tun                 <br /><br /><br />
Block, Xi Xie Po Block, Shen Jia Pu Block of Zao Yuan Oil Field, Xi Bei Block of Xiao Ji Oil Field,       <br /><br /><br />
Duan Nan Block of Duan Liu Bo Oil Field, and Ye San Bo Oil Field, covering a total area of Ninety         <br /><br /><br />
Point Five (90.5) square kilometers, as marked out by the geographic location and the coordinates of      <br /><br /><br />
the connecting points of the boundary lines shown on Annex I attached hereto.                             <br /><br /><br />
3.2    Within the pilot test period, the Pilot Test Area and the specific location map of the             <br /><br /><br />
Pilot Test Area will be shown on the pilot test program.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Any change in the Pilot Test Area shall be proposed by the Contractor, adopted by JMC                     <br /><br /><br />
through discussions and determined upon CNPC's approval. The area other than die Pilot Test Area          <br /><br /><br />
shall continue to be managed by CNPC itself and shall be retained for the Contractor until the            <br /><br /><br />
expiration of the pilot test period.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Within the development period and production period as specified in Article 4.4 and Article               <br /><br /><br />
4.5 hereof, the Development and the Production Area shall be reduced in accordance with Article 5         <br /><br /><br />
under this Contract.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
3.3    In respect of cooperative exploration, development and production for unknown                      <br /><br /><br />
and/or newly-discovered reservoir(s) or payzone(s) below the base of the Kongdian group within the        <br /><br /><br />
Contract Area, after the approval of the Department or Unit, the Parties sliall hold friendly             <br /><br /><br />
negotiations in accordance with the principles of the Model Contract for the Risk Exploration Blocks      <br /><br /><br />
for the Second Round of Invitation for Bids for the Exploitation of Land Petroleum Resources of the       <br /><br /><br />
People’s Republic of China in Cooperation with Foreign Enterprises to sign another Petroleum              <br /><br /><br />
contract after reaching agreement.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
3.4    Except for the rights as expressly provided by the Contract, no right is granted in                <br /><br /><br />
favor of the Contractor to the surface area, subsurface area, lake bed, stream bed and subsoil or any     <br /><br /><br />
natural resources other than Petroleum existing therein, and any things under the surface within the      <br /><br /><br />
Contract Area.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                                                      Article 4                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                   Contract Term                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
4.1 The term of the Contract shall include a pilot test period, a development period and a                                                    <br /><br /><br />
production period.                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
4.2    The pilot test period shall be three (3) consecutive Contract Years, beginning on the                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Date of Commencement of Implementation of the Contract.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
4.3    Where time is insufficient to complete the evaluation work and/or the preparation and                                                  <br /><br /><br />
application for approval of the Overall Development Program before the expiration of the pilot test                                           <br /><br /><br />
period, the pilot test period as described in Article 4.2 herein shall be extended. The period of                                             <br /><br /><br />
extension shall be subject to the approval of CNPC and shall be a reasonable period of time required                                          <br /><br /><br />
to complete the above-mentioned evaluation work and/or the preparation for the Overall Development                                            <br /><br /><br />
Program until the Department or Unit approves or finally rejects the Overall Development Program.                                             <br /><br /><br />
The period of extension shall not exceed six (6) months unless otherwise agreed by the Parties.                                               <br /><br /><br />
4.4    The development period of the Oil Field shall begin on the date of approval by the                                                     <br /><br /><br />
Department or Unit of the Overall Development Program of the said Oil Field, and end on the date of                                           <br /><br /><br />
the entire completion of the Development Operations set forth in the Overall Development Program.                                             <br /><br /><br />
The development period shall not include the time for carrying out additional development                                                     <br /><br /><br />
projects in the production period in accordance with Article 11.5 hereof.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
4.5    The production period of the Oil Field shall be twenty (20) consecutive production                                                     <br /><br /><br />
years beginning on the Date of Commencement of Commercial Production of the said Oil Field,                                                   <br /><br /><br />
unless otherwise provided in Article 4.6.1 herein or Article 25 hereof. Under such circumstances as                                           <br /><br /><br />
where the construction of the Oil Field is to be conducted on a large scale, and the time span required                                       <br /><br /><br />
therefore is long, or where separate production of each of the multiple oil producing zones of the Oil                                        <br /><br /><br />
Field is required, or under other special circumstances, the production period thereof shall, when it is                                      <br /><br /><br />
necessary, be properly extended with the approval of the Department or Unit.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
4.6    Suspension or abandonment of production of the Oil Field                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
4.6.1    Suspension of production from Oil Field within the production period                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
In the event that the Parties agree to suspend temporarily production from the Oil Field which                                                <br /><br /><br />
has entered into commercial production, the Production Area covered by that Oil Field may be                                                  <br /><br /><br />
retained within the Contract Area. In no event shall the period of such retention exceed two (2) years                                        <br /><br /><br />
£and be extended beyond the date of the expiration of the production period of that Oil Field except as                                       <br /><br /><br />
| Otherwise provided in Article 25.4 hereof. The duration of the relevant period of production                                                <br /><br /><br />
" suspension and the arrangement for the maintenance operations during the aforesaid period of                                                <br /><br /><br />
 Suspension shall be proposed by the Operator, and shall be decided by JMC through discussion. With                                           <br /><br /><br />
 respect to the aforesaid Oil Field which has been suspended and retained within the Contract Area, in                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                e event that production is restored during the period of such retention, the production period of that        <br /><br /><br />
 Pfl Field shall be extended correspondingly. In the event that the Parties fail to reach an agreement on                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                ^restoration of production by the expiration of the production suspension period decided by JMC               <br /><br /><br />
                                          ugh discussion, the Party who wishes to restore production shall have the right to restore          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    11                                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿production solely. The other Party may later elect to participate in production but shall have no rights   <br /><br /><br />
or obligations in respect of such Oil Field for the solely restored production period.                     <br /><br /><br />
4.6.2 Abandonment of production from the Oil Field within the production period                            <br /><br /><br />
4.6.2.1    During the production period, either Party to the Contract may propose to abandon               <br /><br /><br />
production from the Oil Field within the Contract Area, provided, however, that prior written notice       <br /><br /><br />
shall be given to the other Party to the Contract. The other Party shall make a response in writing        <br /><br /><br />
within ninety (90) days from the date on which the said notice is received. If the other Party also        <br /><br /><br />
agrees to abandon production from the said Oil Field, the abandonment costs shall be paid by the           <br /><br /><br />
Parties in accordance with their proportions stipulated in Article 13.2.2.2 hereof in such Oil Field.      <br /><br /><br />
The Parties shall abandon such Oil Field in accordance with procedure agreed on by the Parties.            <br /><br /><br />
From the date on which the abandonment is completed, the production period of such Oil Field shall         <br /><br /><br />
be terminated and such Oil Field shall be excluded from the Contract Area.                                 <br /><br /><br />
4.6.2.2    If the Contractor notifies CNPC in writing of its decision to abandon production from           <br /><br /><br />
an Oil Field, while CNPC decides not to abandon production from such Oil Field, then from the date         <br /><br /><br />
on which the Contractor receives CNPC’s written response of its aforesaid decision, namely                 <br /><br /><br />
Abandonment Date, all of the Contractor’s rights and obligations under the Contract in respect of the      <br /><br /><br />
said Oil Field, including, but not limited to, the responsibilities for payment of abandonment cost in     <br /><br /><br />
respect of such Oil Field, shall be terminated automatically, provided that the Contractor shall not       <br /><br /><br />
transfer to CNPC any of the Contractor's debts, liabilities and obligations in respect of the said Oil     <br /><br /><br />
Field. In addition, the Contractor shall undertake its debts, liabilities and obligations under the        <br /><br /><br />
Contract prior to the Abandonment Date. From the Abandonment Date, the production period of the            <br /><br /><br />
said Oil Field shall be terminated and the said Oil Field shall be excluded from the Contract Area.        <br /><br /><br />
4.7 The term of the Contract shall not go beyond thirty (30) consecutive Contract Years                    <br /><br /><br />
from the Date of Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract, unless otherwise stipulated           <br /><br /><br />
hereunder.                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                        Article 5                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                       Relinquishment of the Contract Area                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
5.1    The Contract Area excluding the Development Area shall be relinquished on the date                  <br /><br /><br />
of approval of the Overall Development Program.                                                            <br /><br /><br />
5.2    The Contract Area excluding the Production Area shall be relinquished on the Date of                <br /><br /><br />
Commencement of Commercial Production.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
5.3    Within ninety (90) days prior to date of each relinquishment of the Contract Area, the              <br /><br /><br />
Contractor shall submit to CNPC a report on the areas to be relinquished, including a map showing          <br /><br /><br />
the areas to be relinquished with the geographic location and the coordinates of the connecting points     <br /><br /><br />
of the boundary lines. The final map shall be submitted to CNPC on or before the date of                   <br /><br /><br />
relinquishment.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                                                                         Article 6                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            Minimum Pilot Test Work Commitment                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                       and Expected Minimum Pilot Test Expenditures                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
6.1    The Contractor shall prepare the pilot test program within forty-five (45) days after                                                           <br /><br /><br />
the Date of Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract, shall begin to perform the Pilot                                                       <br /><br /><br />
Test Operations within three (3) months after the Date of Commencement of the Implementation of                                                        <br /><br /><br />
the Contract and shall begin the site operation within six (6) months after the Date of Commencement                                                   <br /><br /><br />
of the Implementation of the Contract unless otherwise agreed by the Parties.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
6.2    The Contractor shall fulfill the minimum pilot test work commitment and expected                                                                <br /><br /><br />
minimum pilot test expenditures in accordance with the following provisions:                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
6.2.1 The minimum pilot test work commitment includes the items as follows:                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(1)    In the Duan Nan Block, drill, complete and equip three (3) wells for production; re¬                                                            <br /><br /><br />
enter and recomplete well Guan 167 as a production well; drill and complete one well for water                                                         <br /><br /><br />
injection purposes; design and carry out two well fracture stimulation programs and construct surface                                                  <br /><br /><br />
production testing and treating facilities.                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(2)    Inject water and produce the four (4) production wells to establish as a minimum,                                                               <br /><br /><br />
benchmark rates of production and decline, injectivity rates and pressures, and treating and gathering                                                 <br /><br /><br />
criteria.                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(3) Complete an evaluation of the detailed geology and reservoir engineering for the                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
reservoirs or payzones to determine the optimal production method, including oil analysis by a                                                         <br /><br /><br />
qualified agency to determine true wax content expressed as a weight percent.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(4)    In each of the Shen Jia Pu, Zi Lai Tun, Xiao Ji and Ye San Bo Blocks, commit to an                                                              <br /><br /><br />
expenditure in aggregate of Seven Hundred Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$700,000) for engineering,                                                          <br /><br /><br />
pressure or pump tests, seismic shooting or reprocessing or other technical evaluations as may be                                                      <br /><br /><br />
required to further evaluate each block. Minimum individual block expenditure will not be less than                                                    <br /><br /><br />
One Hundred and Twenty-five Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$125,000).                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                               (5)    Evaluate the latest methods of non-damaging drilling and within fourteen (14) months             <br /><br /><br />
"of commencing Pilot Test Operations, program and commence to drill, complete and test one (1) well                                                    <br /><br /><br />
in Xi Xie Po Block, with a minimum expenditure of Six Hundred Thousand U.S. Dollars                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(US$600,000).                                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                               (6)    At the expiration of the pilot test period, the pilot test appraisal report shall be             <br /><br /><br />
 ibmitted to JMC.                                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                               6.2.2 Prior to the expiration of the pilot test period, if the Contractor opts to enter into the        <br /><br /><br />
                               .elopment period, the Contractor shall formulate the Overall Development Program and complete                           <br /><br /><br />
                      ^application for its approval. This program will also outline the Contractor’s onward commitments                                <br /><br /><br />
                      flic other blocks.                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         14                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿6.2.3    The expected minimum pilot test period expenditures shall be Seven Million Five                     <br /><br /><br />
Hundred Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$7,500,000).                                                                <br /><br /><br />
6.2.4    During the pilot test period, the Contractor shall complete the stipulations of Articles            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
6.2.1 and 6.2.3 and Article 6.2.1 dominates.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
6.3 At the expiration of the pilot test period, the Contractor shall have the following                      <br /><br /><br />
options:                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(1)    to enter into the development period; or                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(2)    to terminate the Contract.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
. 6.4 If, at the expiration of the pilot test period, the actual pilot test work commitment and              <br /><br /><br />
the relevant pilot test expenditures the Contractor has fulfilled exceeds the minimum pilot test work        <br /><br /><br />
and the pilot test expenditures stipulated in Articles 6.2.1 and 6.2.3 herein, the Contractor shall bear     <br /><br /><br />
the excess part of the pilot test expenditures.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
6.5 At the expiration of the pilot test period, if the pilot test work commitment actually                   <br /><br /><br />
fulfilled by the Contractor is less than the minimum pilot test work commitment set forth, regardless        <br /><br /><br />
of whether the expected minimum pilot test expenditures are fulfilled or not fulfilled, whether the          <br /><br /><br />
Contractor opts to enter into die development period under Article 6.3(1) herein or to terminate the         <br /><br /><br />
Contract under Article 6.3(2) herein, the Contractor shall, within thirty (30) days from the date of the     <br /><br /><br />
expiration of the pilot test period, pay CNPC only any unfulfilled balance of the minimum pilot test         <br /><br /><br />
work commitment in U.S. Dollars after it has been converted into a cash equivalent using the method          <br /><br /><br />
provided in Annex II-Accounting Procedure hereto. However, if the minimum pilot test work                    <br /><br /><br />
commitment for the pilot test period is fulfilled while its expected corresponding minimum pilot test        <br /><br /><br />
expenditures are not fulfilled, the unfulfilled part shall be deemed as a saving and shall not be paid to    <br /><br /><br />
CNPC.                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                                                Article 7                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                   Management Organization and Its Functions                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
7.1    For the purpose of the proper performance of the Petroleum Operations, the Parties                                                     <br /><br /><br />
shall establish a Joint Management Committee (JMC) within forty-five (45) days from the Date of                                               <br /><br /><br />
Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract.                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
7.1.1    CNPC and the Contractor shall each appoint an equal number of representatives,                                                       <br /><br /><br />
three (3). to form JMC, and each Party to the Contract shall designate one of its representatives as its                                      <br /><br /><br />
chief representative. Each company comprising the Contractor may appoint one (1) representative.                                              <br /><br /><br />
Either Party may replace any of its representatives, or designate another representative as its chief                                         <br /><br /><br />
representative, by a written notice to the other Party, pursuant to Article 8.2 hereof. All the aforesaid                                     <br /><br /><br />
representatives shall have the right to present their views on the proposals at the meetings held by                                          <br /><br /><br />
JMC. When a decision is to be made on any proposal, the chief representative from each Party to the                                           <br /><br /><br />
Contract shall be the spokesman on behalf of the Party to the Contract.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
The chairman of JMC shall be the chief representative designated by CNPC, and the vice                                                        <br /><br /><br />
chairman shall be the chief representative designated by the Contractor. The chairman of JMC shall                                            <br /><br /><br />
preside over meetings of JMC. In his absence, one representative present at the meeting from CNPC                                             <br /><br /><br />
shall be designated to act as the chairman of the meeting. In the absence of the vice chairman of JMC,                                        <br /><br /><br />
one representative present at the meeting from the Contractor shall be designated to act as the vice                                          <br /><br /><br />
chairman of the meeting. The Parties may, according to need, designate a reasonable number of                                                 <br /><br /><br />
advisers who may attend, but shall not be entitled to vote at, JMC meetings.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
7.1.2    A regular meeting of JMC shall be held at least once a Calendar Quarter, and other                                                   <br /><br /><br />
meetings, if necessary, may be held at any time at the request of any Party to the Contract, upon                                             <br /><br /><br />
giving reasonable notice to the other Party of the date, time and location of the meeting and the items                                       <br /><br /><br />
to be discussed. JMC representatives may attend meetings of the JMC by telephone conference call.                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                           7.2    The Parties shall empower JMC to:                                                           <br /><br /><br />
7.2.1 review and adopt the Work Programs and budgets proposed by the Operator and                                                             <br /><br /><br />
subsequent amendments thereto;                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                           7.2.2    review and adopt the pilot test program and submit it to CNPC for confirmation;           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                           7.2.3    review and adopt the appraisal reports of the development geology and reservoir           <br /><br /><br />
^engineering for the reservoirs or payzones within the Contract Area provided by the Operator;                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                           7.2.4    review and adopt the Overall Development Program and budget for the Oil Field and         <br /><br /><br />
the amendments to the budget;                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                           7.2.5    approve or confirm the following items of procurement and expenditures:                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 (a) approve procurement of any item within the budget with a unit price exceeding Five                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 dred Thousand U.S. Dollars (U.S.$500,000) and any single purchase order of total monetary                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                   exceeding Two Million U.S. Dollars (U.S.$2,000,000);                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                          16                                                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿    (b)    approve a lease of equipment, or an engineering subcontract or a service contract                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
    within the budget of a monetary value exceeding One Million U.S. Dollars (U.S.$ 1,000,000); and                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
    (c)    confirm excess expenditures pursuant to Article 10.2.1 hereof and the expenditures                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
    pursuant to Article 10.2.2 hereof.                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
    7.2.6    propose and announce the Date of Commencement of Commercial Production of the                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
    Oil Field within the Contract Area;                                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
    7.2.7    determine the type and scope of information and data provided to any Third Party and                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
    Affiliate in relation to the Petroleum Operations in accordance with Article 22.5 hereof;                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
    7.2.8    demarcate boundaries of the Development Area and the Production Area of the Oil                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
    Field;                                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
    7.2.9    review and approve the insurance program proposed by the Operator and emergency                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
    procedures on safety and environmental protection;                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
    7.2.10    review and approve personnel training programs;                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
    7.2.11    review and approve minutes and/or resolutions of JMC meetings, and discuss, review,                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
M-  decide and approve other matters that have been proposed by either Party to the Contract or submitted                                                               <br /><br /><br />
    by the expert groups pursuant to Article 7.4.2 hereof or by the Operator; and                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
    7.2.12    review and examine matters required to be submitted to relevant authorities of the                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
    Chinese Government and/or CNPC for approval.                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
    7.3    Decisions of JMC shall be made unanimously through consultation. All decisions                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
    made unanimously shall be deemed as formal decisions and shall be equally binding upon the Parties.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
    When matters upon which agreement cannot be reached arise, the Parties may convene another                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
    meeting in an attempt to find a new solution thereto based on the principle of mutual benefit. If it is                                                             <br /><br /><br />
    considered by the chairman and/or the vice chairman or their nominees that a matter requires urgent                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
    jjandiing or may be decided without convening a meeting, JMC may make decisions through telexes,                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                             les or the circulation of documents.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                     7.4    JMC shall establish the following subordinate bodies:                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                     7.4.1 Secretariat                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                     The secretariat shall be a permanent organization consisting of two (2) secretaries. One                           <br /><br /><br />
     taiy shall be appointed by each of the Parties. The secretaries shall not be members of JMC, but                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
     attend meetings of JMC as observers. The duties of the secretariat are as follows:                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                     f (a) to keep minutes of meetings;                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                           to prepare summaries of the resolutions for JMC meetings;                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                           to draft and transmit notices of meetings; and                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                             to receive and transmit proposal, reports or plans, etc. submitted by the Operator                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                             ‘sed by any Party to the Contract, that require discussion, review or approval by JMC.                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          17                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                     yd <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿7.4.2 Expert Groups                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Advisory expert groups shall be established in accordance with the requirements of the                      <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations in various periods. Each expert group shall consist of an equal number of              <br /><br /><br />
CNPC Personnel and the Contractor’s employee, and with the agreement of JMC, any other                      <br /><br /><br />
personnel. JMC shall discuss and decide upon their establishment or dissolution, size, tasks, location      <br /><br /><br />
of their work and the appointment of their leaders in accordance with the requirements of their work.       <br /><br /><br />
The expert groups shall have the following functions:                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(a)    to discuss and study matters assigned to them by JMC and submitted by the Operator                   <br /><br /><br />
to JMC for its review and approval and any other matter assigned to them by JMC and to make                 <br /><br /><br />
constructive suggestions to JMC;                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(b)    to have access to and observe and investigate the Petroleum Operations conducted by                  <br /><br /><br />
the Operator at its office and operating sites as work requires and to submit relevant reports to JMC;      <br /><br /><br />
and,                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(c) to attend meetings of JMC as observers at the request of JMC.                                           <br /><br /><br />
7.5 When one of the companies comprising the Contractor acts as the Operator, CNPC                          <br /><br /><br />
shall have the right to assign five (5) professional representatives to the Operator's administrative and   <br /><br /><br />
technical departments which are related to the Petroleum Operations, who may work at length                 <br /><br /><br />
together with the Operator's staff. The Operator's staff shall regularly discuss their work with the        <br /><br /><br />
professional representatives of CNPC.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
The professional representatives shall have access to the centers of research, design, and data             <br /><br /><br />
processing related only to the execution of the Contract and to the operating sites to observe all the      <br /><br /><br />
activities and study all the information with respect to the Petroleum Operations. Whether to provide       <br /><br /><br />
such access to the aforesaid centers outside the People's Republic of China shall be decided by JMC         <br /><br /><br />
through discussion. If the decision is made, such access shall be arranged by the Operator and the          <br /><br /><br />
Operator shall use all reasonable endeavors to assist the professional representatives to have access to    <br /><br /><br />
Third Parties' sites. The work of professional representatives of CNPC shall be arranged by the             <br /><br /><br />
manager(s) of the departments of the Operator in which professional representatives work.                   <br /><br /><br />
Professional representatives of CNPC, except for the professional representatives in charge of              <br /><br /><br />
procurement who shall undertake their functions in accordance with Article 7.6 herein, shall not            <br /><br /><br />
interfere in the decision making on relevant matters by departmental managers) of the Operator.             <br /><br /><br />
However, such professional representatives shall have the right to make proposals and comments to           <br /><br /><br />
departmental managers) of the Operator or to report directly to CNPC's representatives in JMC.              <br /><br /><br />
When CNPC acts as the Operator, the Contractor may also assign professional representatives                 <br /><br /><br />
including professional representatives in charge of procurement.                                            <br /><br /><br />
7.5.1    On the principle of mutual cooperation and coordination, the Operator shall provide                <br /><br /><br />
the professional representatives with necessary facilities and assistance to perform office work and to     <br /><br /><br />
observe the operating sites, etc.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
7.5.2    The number of professional representatives shall be decided by JMC through                         <br /><br /><br />
consultations.                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />

construction companies and enterprises in China which can provide services and undertake                       <br /><br /><br />

enterprises concerned both inside and outside China, and the work of calling for bids shall be done            <br /><br /><br />
within the territory of China.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />

the Operator on the determination of award of contracts and to participate in negotiations for                 <br /><br /><br />
subcontracts and services contracts.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
Operator and the professional representatives of CNPC in charge of procurement sliall, in accordance           <br /><br /><br />
with the provisions specified in Article 7.6.2 herein, define those items which are to be procured in          <br /><br /><br />
the People's Republic of China and those items which are to be procured abroad.                                <br /><br /><br />
