﻿ Article 8                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 Operator                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

8.1    The Parties agree that Pan-China Resources Ltd. shall act as the Operator for the                 <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations within die Contract Area, unless otherwise stipulated in Article 8.9 herein and     <br /><br /><br />
Article 30.5 hereof.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
The Operator shall start to deal with the relevant matters concerning the site operation within          <br /><br /><br />
thirty (30) days before the commencement of the pilot test site operations and the relevant matters      <br /><br /><br />
concerning the Development Operations within forty-five (45) days before the beginning of the            <br /><br /><br />
Development Operations; and shall reach agreements with CNPC's relevant departments respectively         <br /><br /><br />
and jointly make corresponding arrangements.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
8.2    The names, positions and resumes of the staff and organization chart of the Operator              <br /><br /><br />
shall be submitted in advance to CNPC and the appointment of the Operator's senior staff must be         <br /><br /><br />
subject to the consent of the Parties.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
8.3    The Operator shall have the following obligations:                                                <br /><br /><br />
8.3.1    To apply the appropriate and advanced technology and business managerial                        <br /><br /><br />
experience to perform the Petroleum Operations reasonably, economically and efficiently in               <br /><br /><br />
accordance with sound international practice.                                                            <br /><br /><br />
8.3.2    To prepare Work Programs and budgets related to the Petroleum Operations and to                 <br /><br /><br />
carry out the approved Work Programs and budgets.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
8.3.3    To be responsible for procurement of installations, equipment, and supplies and                 <br /><br /><br />
entering into subcontracts and service contracts related to the Petroleum Operations, in accordance      <br /><br /><br />
with the approved Work Programs and budgets and the applicable provisions of Articles 7.2.5,7.6 and      <br /><br /><br />
10.2 hereof.                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
8.3.4    To prepare in advance, in accordance with Article 16 hereof, a personnel training               <br /><br /><br />
program and budget before the commencement of the Pilot Test Operations, the Development                 <br /><br /><br />
Operations and Production Operations respectively, and, in accordance with the said program and          <br /><br /><br />
budget, to be responsible for preparing an annual personnel training program and budget and carrying     <br /><br /><br />
out die annual program and budget after approval by JMC.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
8.3.5    To establish an insurance program, and to enter into and implement the insurance                <br /><br /><br />
contracts in accordance with Article 21 hereof.                                                          <br /><br /><br />
8.3.6    To issue cash-call notices to all the Parties to the Contract to raise the required funds       <br /><br /><br />
based on the approved budgets and in accordance with Article 12 hereof and Anaex II-Accounting           <br /><br /><br />
Procedure hereto.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
8.3.7    To maintain complete and accurate accounting records of all the costs and                       <br /><br /><br />
expenditures of the Petroleum Operations in accordance with the provisions of Annex II -Accounting       <br /><br /><br />
Procedure hereto and to keep the accounting books secure and in good order.                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                            21                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿8.3.8    To make necessary preparation for regular meetings of JMC and to submit in advance                 <br /><br /><br />
to JMC necessary information related to the matters to be reviewed and approved by JMC.                     <br /><br /><br />
8.3.9    To inform directly or indirectly all the Subcontractors which render services for the              <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations in China and all the Expatriate Employees of the Operator and of                       <br /><br /><br />
Subcontractors who are engaged in the Petroleum Operations in China that they shall be subject to the       <br /><br /><br />
laws, decrees, and other rules and regulations of the People's Republic of China.                           <br /><br /><br />
8.3.10    To report its work to JMC as provided in Article 7.2 hereof.                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
8.4    In the course of the performance of the Petroleum Operations, any loss arising out of                <br /><br /><br />
the gross negligence or willful misconduct of the Operator or the employees of the Operator shall be        <br /><br /><br />
borne solely by the Operator. The Operator shall make its best efforts in accordance with international     <br /><br /><br />
petroleum industry practice to include provisions similar to this Article 8.4 herein in related             <br /><br /><br />
subcontracts and service contracts.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
8.5    In the course of the performance of the Petroleum Operations, the Operator shall                     <br /><br /><br />
handle the information, samples or reports in accordance with the following provisions:                     <br /><br /><br />
8.5.1    The Operator shall provide CNPC with various information, samples and data, which                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
are obtained in the course of the Petroleum Operations in accordance with Articles 19 and 25 of the         <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Regulations and Annex V - Data Control hereto. The ownership of all the information,              <br /><br /><br />
samples and data shall vest in CNPC; and the Operator shall have the right to use and handle such           <br /><br /><br />
information, samples and data in accordance with Annex V - Data Control hereto. The Contractor              <br /><br /><br />
shall have the right to obtain the copies of the aforesaid information, samples and data. The               <br /><br /><br />
information and data shall be reported to CNPC at the same time that the Contractor reports them to         <br /><br /><br />
its parent corporation. Upon receipt by the Contractor of any report from its parent corporation            <br /><br /><br />
concerning such information and data, a copy of such report shall be furnished to CNPC as soon as           <br /><br /><br />
practicable.                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
8.5.2    The Operator shall furnish respectively CNPC and the Contractor in a timely manner                 <br /><br /><br />
with reports on safety, environmental protection and accidents related to the Petroleum Operations          <br /><br /><br />
and with financial reports prepared in accordance with the provisions of Annex II - Accounting              <br /><br /><br />
Procedure hereto.                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
8.5.3    The Operator shall, at the request of any Party to the Contract, furnish that Party to             <br /><br /><br />
the Contract with the following:                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
8.5.3.1    procurement plans for purchasing equipment and materials, inquiries, offers, orders              <br /><br /><br />
and service contracts, etc.;                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
8.5.3.2    technical manuals, technical specifications, design criteria, design documents                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(including design drawings), construction records and information, consumption statistics, equipment        <br /><br /><br />
inventory, spare parts inventory, etc.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
8.5.3.3    technical investigation and cost analysis reports; and                                           <br /><br /><br />
8.5.3.4    other information relating to the Petroleum Operations already acquired by the                   <br /><br /><br />
Operator in the performance of the Contract.                                                                <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                   22                                                     1                                 <br /><br /><br />
﻿8.6    In the course of performing the Petroleum Operations, the Operator shall abide by the                 <br /><br /><br />
laws, decrees, standards and other rules and regulations with respect to environmental protection and        <br /><br /><br />
safety of the People's Republic of China and shall endeavor in accordance with the international             <br /><br /><br />
petroleum industry practice to:                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
8.6.1    minimize the damage and destruction caused by the Petroleum Operations to                           <br /><br /><br />
environments, community and ecological environment, and prevent land, forests, vegetation, crops,            <br /><br /><br />
buildings and other installations from being damaged and destroyed;                                          <br /><br /><br />
8.6.2    control blowouts promptly and prevent or avoid waste or loss of Petroleum                           <br /><br /><br />
discovered in or produced from the Contract Area;                                                            <br /><br /><br />
8.6.3    prevent Petroleum from flowing into low pressure formations or damaging adjacent                    <br /><br /><br />
petroleum-bearing formations, and prevent water from flowing into petroleum-bearing formations               <br /><br /><br />
through dry holes or other wells, except for the purpose of secondary recovery; and                          <br /><br /><br />
8.6.4    minimize the danger to personnel safety and health.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
8.7    With a view to efficiently conducting Work Programs approved by JMC, the                              <br /><br /><br />
Operator may lease and/or use land with compensation therefore and to obtain rights of way subject to        <br /><br /><br />
Chinese laws and regulations. Any costs incurred by the Operator for this purpose shall be                   <br /><br /><br />
respectively charged to Development Costs and Operating Costs having regard to the date on which             <br /><br /><br />
the same are actually incurred.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
8.8    Project Management Team                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
For the development of the Oil Field within the Contract Area, a project management team                     <br /><br /><br />
(hereafter referred to as “PMT”) may be established after mutual discussion for the development of           <br /><br /><br />
such Oil Field in the organization of the Operator within thirty (30) days from the date of approval of      <br /><br /><br />
the Overall Development Program for the said Field by the Department or Unit. PMT shall exist for            <br /><br /><br />
the period of the development of the said Oil Field.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
PMT shall comprise those personnel designated by the Parties and the number of CNPC's                        <br /><br /><br />
personnel shall be no less than one third (1/3) of the total number of personnel within PMT. The             <br /><br /><br />
Contractor shall designate a person acting as the manager of PMT, and CNPC shall designate a person          <br /><br /><br />
acting as the deputy manager of PMT.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
PMT shall be located at the Operator's office within the Chinese territory. The working                      <br /><br /><br />
locations) of the members of PMT shall be decided according to the need of the work.                         <br /><br /><br />
The specific organization, staffing and working system of PMT and responsibilities and                       <br /><br /><br />
competence of various positions including those of CNPC's personnel assigned to PMT shall be                 <br /><br /><br />
determined by the Parties through consultation prior to the approval of the Overall Development              <br /><br /><br />
Program for the said Oil Field.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
All costs for PMT shall be borne by the Operator, and shall be charged to the Development                    <br /><br /><br />
Costs.                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />

 8.9 Transfer and take over of the Production Operations                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                         \                   <br /><br /><br />
                              23                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
﻿Before the full recovery of the Development Costs actually incurred in accordance with the                 <br /><br /><br />
Overall Development Program of the Oil Field within the Contract Area, CNPC may, after agreement           <br /><br /><br />
reached through consultations of JMC, take over the Production Operations of that Oil Field, if            <br /><br /><br />
conditions permit. After the full recovery of the Development Costs actually incurred in accordance        <br /><br /><br />
with the Overall Development Program of the Oil Field within the Contract Area, CNPC shall, at any         <br /><br /><br />
time, have the right by giving a written notice to the Contractor to take over the Production              <br /><br /><br />
Operations. Both aforesaid cases shall be effected in accordance with the procedures described             <br /><br /><br />
hereunder.                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
8.9.1    The Contractor acting as the Operator shall submit a transfer plan of the Production              <br /><br /><br />
Operations to CNPC and JMC respectively within sixty (60) days following the date of receiving the         <br /><br /><br />
written notice from CNPC. Such transfer plan shall include, but not be limited to, a list of various       <br /><br /><br />
posts to be taken over by CNPC, a schedule of transfer by stages, inventories of the relevant facilities   <br /><br /><br />
and equipment and an inventory of all documents, manuals, data and information necessary for the           <br /><br /><br />
Production Operations. Where the transfer of some of the Production Operations involves any Third          <br /><br /><br />
Party, the Contractor acting as the Operator shall consult with CNPC in advance and propose a              <br /><br /><br />
solution thereto in the transfer plan, however, this situation shall not be taken by the Contractor acting <br /><br /><br />
as the Operator as an excuse to delay and hinder the transfer of the Production Operations.                <br /><br /><br />
JMC shall, within thirty (30) days after receiving the said plan, review and approve it.                   <br /><br /><br />
8.9.2    CNPC shall, within sixty (60) days from the date of receiving the transfer plan of the            <br /><br /><br />
Production Operations approved by JMC, submit to the Contractor and JMC respectively the lists and         <br /><br /><br />
resumes of CNPC's personnel who will take over the posts. The personnel named in the lists shall be        <br /><br /><br />
persons who have been trained by the Contractor in accordance with the provisions set forth in Article     <br /><br /><br />
16 hereof or personnel who are considered by CNPC to be competent. Within one hundred and eighty           <br /><br /><br />
(180) days from the date of receiving CNPC's lists of the personnel who will take over the posts, the      <br /><br /><br />
Contractor acting as the Operator shall arrange for such personnel to undergo step by step practical       <br /><br /><br />
training for the posts to be taken over by them and shall assist CNPC to administer a qualification test   <br /><br /><br />
for such personnel.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
8.9.3    Within three hundred and thirty (330) days from the date of receiving the written                 <br /><br /><br />
notice from CNPC, the Contractor acting as the Operator shall submit to JMC a report on the                <br /><br /><br />
completion of preparations for the transfer of the Production Operations. Such report shall include the    <br /><br /><br />
results of the qualification test for CNPC's personnel who will take over the Production Operations        <br /><br /><br />
and shall be confirmed by JMC within thirty (30) days after the receipt of the said report. The transfer   <br /><br /><br />
of the Production Operations shall begin on the date when JMC makes such confirmation.                     <br /><br /><br />
8.9.3.1    When the completion of preparations for the transfer of the Production Operations is            <br /><br /><br />
confirmed by JMC, the Contractor acting as the Operator shall, in accordance with the transfer             <br /><br /><br />
schedule by stages, transfer to CNPC’s take-over personnel control of all facilities and equipment         <br /><br /><br />
relating to the Production Operations in the Oil Field, and all documents, manuals, data and               <br /><br /><br />
information regarding the use and operation of such facilities and equipment, so that CNPC's               <br /><br /><br />
personnel are able to manage and handle such facilities and equipment.                                     <br /><br /><br />
8.9.3.2    If JMC believes that preparations for the transfer of the Production Operations have            <br /><br /><br />
not been completed and sets another deadline for the completion of preparations for the transfer of the    <br /><br /><br />
Production Operations, the preparations for the transfer shall be completed prior to the deadline and      <br /><br /><br />
the transfer shall begin thereafter.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
﻿8.9.4    The transfer in respect of the accounting and financial aspects shall be handled in                 <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Annex II-Accounting Procedure hereto.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
8.9.5    During the preparation for the transfer of the Production Operations and in the course              <br /><br /><br />
of the actual transfer, the Contractor acting as the Operator shall perform the functions and obligations    <br /><br /><br />
provided for in Articles 8.3,8.4,8.5 and 8.6 herein in respect of the Oil Field undergoing the transfer of   <br /><br /><br />
the Production Operations, until the date when CNPC has completely assumed control of and taken              <br /><br /><br />
over the Production Operations of the Oil Field. Thereafter, the functions and obligations of the            <br /><br /><br />
Operator provided for in Articles 8.3,8.4,8.5 and 8.6 herein shall be by analogy applicable to CNPC.         <br /><br /><br />
8.9.6    After CNPC has taken over the Production Operations and become the Operator of                      <br /><br /><br />
the Oil Field, the Contractor shall still have the obligation, pursuant to Article 2 hereof to provide       <br /><br /><br />
CNPC with the relevant technical and personnel training assistance, and the costs incurred thereby           <br /><br /><br />
shall be charged to the Operating Costs in accordance with the provisions of Annex II-Accounting             <br /><br /><br />
Procedure hereto.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
8.9.7    When CNPC takes over the Production Operations in the Oil Field, the CNPC                           <br /><br /><br />
personnel employed by the Contractor acting as the Operator for the Production Operations of the said        <br /><br /><br />
Oil Field shall be transferred to CNPC's employment. If CNPC needs to retain the service of any of           <br /><br /><br />
the Expatriate Employees employed by the Contractor acting as the Operator or the Contractor still           <br /><br /><br />
needs to keep some of CNPC Personnel in its employment, an agreement shall be reached through                <br /><br /><br />
consultation between the Parties prior to the transfer.                                                      <br /><br /><br />
8.9.8    The expenses incurred in the transfer and takeover of the Production Operations shall               <br /><br /><br />
be charged to the Operating Costs.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                          Article 9                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                              Assistance Provided by CNPC                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
9.1    To enable the Contractor to carry out expeditiously and efficiently the Petroleum                     <br /><br /><br />
Operations, CNPC shall have the obligation to assist the Contractor at its request to:                       <br /><br /><br />
9.1.1    obtain the approvals or permits needed to open accounts with Bank of China;                         <br /><br /><br />
9.1.2    go through the formalities of exchanging foreign currencies;                                        <br /><br /><br />
9.1.3    obtain office space, office supplies, transportation and communication facilities and               <br /><br /><br />
make arrangements for accommodation as required;                                                             <br /><br /><br />
9.1.4 go through the formalities of Customs;                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
9.1.5    obtain entry and exit visas for the Expatriate Employees who will come to China for                 <br /><br /><br />
the performance of Contract and for their dependents who will visit them or reside in China for a long       <br /><br /><br />
period and provide assistance for their transportation and moving as well as medical services and            <br /><br /><br />
travel in China;                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
9.1.6    obtain necessary permission to send abroad, if necessary, documents, data, oil, and                 <br /><br /><br />
other samples for analysis or processing during the performance of the Petroleum Operations; and             <br /><br /><br />
9.1.7    contact and coordinate with departments engaged in fishing, aquatic product, stock                  <br /><br /><br />
raising, agriculture, meteorology, ocean shipping, civil aviation, railway, transportation, electric         <br /><br /><br />
power, communication and services for supply bases, etc. for relevant matters and otherwise assist the       <br /><br /><br />
Contractor in obtaining on a timely basis approvals necessary for the conduct of the Petroleum               <br /><br /><br />
Operations under the Contract;                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
9.1.8    lease or use warehouses, yards, terminal facilities, barges, aircraft, pipelines and land,          <br /><br /><br />
etc. in the implementation of the Petroleum Operations; and                                                  <br /><br /><br />
9.1.9    facilitate Contractor’s and the Subcontractors' registration in China.                              <br /><br /><br />
9.2    In accordance with Article 15 hereof, CNPC shall, at the request of the Contractor,                   <br /><br /><br />
assist the Contractor with the recruitment of Chinese Personnel.                                             <br /><br /><br />
9.3    CNPC shall, at the request of the Contractor, sell to the Contractor all available data               <br /><br /><br />
and samples, including oil samples for export, concerning the Contract Area other than those                 <br /><br /><br />
produced as a result of Petroleum Operations hereunder in accordance with any relevant rules and             <br /><br /><br />
regulations and CNPC shall also assist the Contractor to arrange the purchase of any environmental,          <br /><br /><br />
hydrological, meteorological data, etc. from the relevant departments in China for reasonable prices.        <br /><br /><br />
9.4    CNPC shall, at the request of the Contractor, also assist the Contractor with matters                 <br /><br /><br />
other than those under Articles 9.1, 9.2 and 9.3 herein if possible, including, but not limited to           <br /><br /><br />
assisting the Contractor to obtain favorable treatments that may be available from time to time from         <br /><br /><br />
the relevant tax, customs, investment, registration and other governmental authorities of China.             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                       26                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿9.5 All expenses incurred in the assistance provided by CNPC in accordance with this                  <br /><br /><br />
Article 9 shall be paid by the Contractor and shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of   <br /><br /><br />
Annex E-Accounting Procedure hereto. The Contractor shall pay to CNPC One Hundred Thousand            <br /><br /><br />
US Dollars (US$100,000) per year during the pilot test period for the assistance provided by CNPC.    <br /><br /><br />
During the development period and the production period, the Contractor shall pay to CNPC for the     <br /><br /><br />
assistance provided by CNPC in accordance with Article 5.2.14.3 of Annex E-Accounting Procedure       <br /><br /><br />
hereto.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                           Article 10                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                               Work Program and Budget                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
10.1    After the Date of Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract, the                            <br /><br /><br />
Operator shall propose and submit to JMC the annual Work Program and budget for the remainder of             <br /><br /><br />
the same Calendar Year at the first regular meeting of JMC. Before the fifteenth (15th) of September         <br /><br /><br />
of each Calendar Year, the Operator shall complete and submit to JMC for its review an annual Work           <br /><br /><br />
Program and budget for the next Calendar Year except otherwise agreed by CNPC. JMC shall either              <br /><br /><br />
adopt the annual Work Program and budget as submitted or make such modifications agreed by the               <br /><br /><br />
Parties. The adopted annual Work Program and budget shall be submitted to CNPC for review and                <br /><br /><br />
approval within one (1) month as of the date on which they are submitted to JMC. Within fifteen (15)         <br /><br /><br />
days following the receipt of the annual Work Program and budget, CNPC shall notify JMC in writing           <br /><br /><br />
of its approval or disapproval or any modifications thereto with its detailed reasons. If CNPC requests      <br /><br /><br />
any modifications to the aforesaid annual Work Program and budget, the Parties shall promptly hold           <br /><br /><br />
meetings to make modifications and any modifications agreed upon by the Parties shall be effected            <br /><br /><br />
immediately. In case CNPC fails to notify JMC in writing of its approval or disapproval or any               <br /><br /><br />
modification within fifteen (15) days, the annual Work Program and budget adopted by JMC shall be            <br /><br /><br />
deemed to have been approved by CNPC. The Operator shall make its best efforts to perform the                <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations in accordance with the approved or modified annual Work Program and budget.             <br /><br /><br />
As required for reviewing Work Program and budget by JMC, the Operator shall submit to                       <br /><br /><br />
JMC the supporting data as detailed as possible.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
10.2    The Operator may, in accordance with the following provisions, incur excess                          <br /><br /><br />
expenditures or expenditures outside the budget in carrying out the Work Program and budget,                 <br /><br /><br />
provided that the objectives of the approved Work Program and budget are not changed.                        <br /><br /><br />
10.2.1    In carrying out an approved budget for a single item, such as the drilling of a well, the          <br /><br /><br />
Operator may, if necessary, incur excess expenditures of no more than ten percent (10%) of the               <br /><br /><br />
budgeted amount. The Operator shall report quarterly the aggregate amount of all such excess                 <br /><br /><br />
expenditures to JMC for confirmation.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
10.2.2    For the efficient performance of the Petroleum Operations, the Operator may, without               <br /><br /><br />
approval, undertake certain individual projects which are not included in the Work Program and               <br /><br /><br />
budget, for a maximum expenditure of One Hundred Thousand U.S. Dollars (U.S.$100,000), but the               <br /><br /><br />
Operator shall, within ten (10) days after such expenditures are incurred, report to JMC for                 <br /><br /><br />
confirmation. In case of emergency, the Operator may incur emergency expenditures for the amount             <br /><br /><br />
actually needed but shall report such expenditures to JMC as soon as they are made. However, the             <br /><br /><br />
said emergency expenditures shall not be subject to Articles 10.2.3 and 10.2.4 herein.                       <br /><br /><br />
10.2.3    In the event that the aggregate of excess expenditures under Article 10.2.1 herein and             <br /><br /><br />
expenditures under Article 10.2.2 herein incurred in a Calendar Year cause the total expenditures of         <br /><br /><br />
that Calendar Year to exceed the approved annual budget, such excess shall not exceed five percent           <br /><br /><br />
(5%) of the approved annual budget for that Calendar Year. If the aforesaid excess is expected to be         <br /><br /><br />
in excess of five percent (5%) of the annual budget, the Operator shall present its reasons therefore to     <br /><br /><br />
JMC and obtain its approval prior to incurring such expenditures.                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿10.2.4 When JMC confirms the excess expenditures mentioned in Articles 10.2.1 herein and            <br /><br /><br />
the expenditures mentioned in 10.2.2 herein:                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    if expenditures or excess expenditures are determined to be reasonable, the Operator         <br /><br /><br />
may incur such expenditures or excess expenditures again during the same Calendar Year subject to   <br /><br /><br />
Article 10.2 herein; or                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(b)    if expenditures or excess expenditures are determined to be unreasonable, the                <br /><br /><br />
Operator shall not incur such expenditures or excess expenditures again during the same Calendar    <br /><br /><br />
Year and such unreasonable expenditures or excess expenditures shall be dealt with in accordance    <br /><br /><br />
with Article 5.4 of Annex H-Accounting Procedure hereto;                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

 29                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
﻿                              Article 11                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 Preparation of the Overall Development Program                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
11.1    During the pilot test period, if the Operator opts to enter into the development period,                <br /><br /><br />
the Operator shall complete the preparation of the Overall Development Program and submit to JMC                <br /><br /><br />
and CNPC for confirmation. CNPC shall submit the Overall Development Program of the Oil Field                   <br /><br /><br />
to Department or Unit for approval as soon as possible.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
11.2    Prior to the submission of the Overall Development Program, the Operator shall                          <br /><br /><br />
submit to CNPC the report of oil-in-place of the Oil Field and the Environment Impact Statements,               <br /><br /><br />
which shall be entrusted to and prepared by a qualified organization. The aforesaid reports and                 <br /><br /><br />
statements shall be submitted to the competent authorities of the Chinese Government through CNPC               <br /><br /><br />
for review and approval.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
11.3    The Operator shall perform the Development Operations in accordance with the                            <br /><br /><br />
Overall Development Program of the Oil Field approved by the Department or Unit If the Contractor               <br /><br /><br />
acting as the Operator, without adequate justification, fails to commence such Development                      <br /><br /><br />
Operations within ninety (90) days after the date of approval of the Overall Development Program of             <br /><br /><br />
the Oil Field by the Department or Unit, or if an unreasonable delay caused unilaterally by the                 <br /><br /><br />
Contractor acting as the Operator results in a suspension or a halt of ninety (90) continuous days in           <br /><br /><br />
the Development Operations of the Oil Field, CNPC has the right to request the Contractor to resume             <br /><br /><br />
the Development Operations within a reasonable period of time set forth by CNPC; and if the                     <br /><br /><br />
Development Operations fail to be resumed within such period, CNPC has the right to request the                 <br /><br /><br />
Contractor to give up all its rights in the said Oil Field. If CNPC so requests the Contractor, pursuant        <br /><br /><br />
to the provisions of this Article 11.3 herein, to give up all of its rights in the said Oil Field, the          <br /><br /><br />
Contractor shall waive all of its rights in the said Oil Field from the date of receipt by the Contractor       <br /><br /><br />
of the written notice in that regard from CNPC.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
11.4    In the event of the Oil Field Straddling a Boundary, CNPC shall arrange for the                         <br /><br /><br />
Contractor and the neighboring parties involved to work out a unitized Overall Development Program              <br /><br /><br />
for such Oil Field and to help negotiate the relevant provisions thereof.                                       <br /><br /><br />
11.5    The procedures specified in this Article 11 shall be applied, by analogy, to                            <br /><br /><br />
determination of additional development projects in the Oil Field within the Contract Area during the           <br /><br /><br />
production period, such projects being designed as a supplementary to and/or an adjustment of the               <br /><br /><br />
existing Overall Development Program for such Oil Field.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
11.6    If the Parties deem that it is necessary to have appraisal trial production for                         <br /><br /><br />
preparation of the Overall Development Program for the Oil Field within Contract Area, the Parties              <br /><br /><br />
shall reach a written agreement through negotiation on terms and conditions of appraisal trial                  <br /><br /><br />
production which shall be attached hereto as a supplementary document.                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                              30                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                Article 12                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                Financing and Cost Recovery                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
12.1    Funds required for the Petroleum Operations shall be raised by the Operator in                             <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Work Programs and budgets determined pursuant to the relevant provisions of the                    <br /><br /><br />
Contract, the provisions described in Annex II - Accounting Procedure hereto, and the provisions                   <br /><br /><br />
described here below.                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
12.1.1    All the Pilot Test Costs required in the Pilot Test Area shall be provided solely by the                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
Contractor. However, the costs required for the fulfillment of the minimum pilot test work                         <br /><br /><br />
commitment shall be deemed the equity capital of the Contractor.                                                   <br /><br /><br />
12.1.2    All the Development Costs required in the Oil Field within the Contract Area shall be                    <br /><br /><br />
provided solely by the Contractor.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
12.1.3    The Operating Costs incurred for the performance of the Production Operations of the                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
Oil Field before the Date of Commencement of Commercial Production shall be considered as                          <br /><br /><br />
Development Costs. The Operating Costs so incurred after the Date of Commencement of                               <br /><br /><br />
Commercial Production shall be paid respectively by CNPC and the Contractor in accordance with                     <br /><br /><br />
the Parties' proportion of the “investment recovery oil” stipulated in Article 13.2.2.2, namely in                 <br /><br /><br />
proportion of eighteen percent (18%) by CNPC and eighty-two percent (82%) by the Contractor.                       <br /><br /><br />
After the “investment recovery oil” changes into the “allocable remainder oil”, the Operating Costs                <br /><br /><br />
shall be paid respectively by CNPC and the Contractor in accordance with the Parties' proportion of                <br /><br /><br />
the “allocable remainder oil” stipulated in Article 13.2.3, namely in proportion of fifty-one percent              <br /><br /><br />
(51%) by CNPC and forty-nine percent (49%) by the Contractor. However, the Parties agree that                      <br /><br /><br />
CNPC's Operating Costs shall be firstly paid by the Contractor for CNPC and the said proportion of                 <br /><br /><br />
the Operating Costs to be recovered by CNPC pursuant to Article 13.2.2.1 under this Contract shall be              <br /><br /><br />
recovered by the Contractor.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
12.1.4    For the purpose of implementation of the Contract, CNPC shall agree that the                             <br /><br /><br />
Contractor may, when financing, use the entitlement of its share of production under the Contract as a             <br /><br /><br />
security for loans, provided that the Contractor shall apply to CNPC in advance and the application                <br /><br /><br />
therefore shall be examined by CNPC, and provided further that the right and interests of CNPC under               <br /><br /><br />
the Contract shall not be impaired thereby.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
12.2    The Operating Costs for any given Calendar Year actually incurred by CNPC and the                          <br /><br /><br />
Contractor in respect of the Oil Field pursuant to Article 12.1.3 herein, shall be recovered in kind by            <br /><br /><br />
the Parties out of the Crude Oil produced from the said Oil Field during that Calendar Year in                     <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Annex II - Accounting Procedure hereto, after the Operating Costs have been                        <br /><br /><br />
converted into a quantity of Crude Oil on the basis of the Crude Oil price determined in accordance                <br /><br /><br />
with Article 14 hereof. Unrecovered Operating Costs shall be carried forward to the succeeding                     <br /><br /><br />
Calendar Year(s).                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
12.3    The Pilot Test Costs and the Development Costs incurred by the Contractor in                               <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Articles 12.1.1 and 12,1.2 hereof, and all the costs (referred to as Pre-development               <br /><br /><br />
Costs hereinafter) spent by CNPC for exploration and proving the potential commerciality of the                    <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum discovery within the Contract Area and for the wells drilled and surface production                    . <br /><br /><br />
facilities constructed therein before the date of signing of the Contract, shall be recovered in kind out          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                              31                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
﻿of the Crude Oil produced from such Oil Field by the Contractor and CNPC in accordance with            <br /><br /><br />
Article 13.2.2.2 hereof after the Pilot Test Costs, Development Costs and Pre-development Costs have   <br /><br /><br />
been converted into a quantity of Crude Oil based on the Crude Oil price determined in accordance      <br /><br /><br />
with Article 14 hereof.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
12.4 If the Contractor fails to enter into the development period after the Pilot Test                 <br /><br /><br />
Operations, the unrecovered Pilot Test Costs incurred by the Contractor shall be deemed as its loss.   <br /><br /><br />
Under no circumstances shall CNPC reimburse the Contractor for such loss.                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />

 32                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                              Article 13                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                           Crude Oil Production and Allocation                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
13.1    The Operator shall, in accordance with the production profile, adjusted as the case                   <br /><br /><br />
may be set forth in the Overall Development Program for the Oil Field as approved by the Department           <br /><br /><br />
or Unit, work out a Crude Oil production plan for the Oil Field in each Calendar Year and carry out           <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oil production pursuant to such plan.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
13.2    The Annual Gross Production of Crude Oil of the Oil Field within the Contract Area                    <br /><br /><br />
in each Calendar Year during the production period shall be allocated in accordance with the                  <br /><br /><br />
following sequence and proportions:                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
13.2.1    The percentages of the Annual Gross Production of Crude Oil specified in paragraphs                 <br /><br /><br />
(a) and (b) hereunder shall be used for payments of the Value Added Tax and of Royalty respectively           <br /><br /><br />
and shall be paid in kind to the relevant authorities of the Chinese Government through CNPC.                 <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Value Added Tax shall be paid in accordance with relevant regulations of the People's                  <br /><br /><br />
Republic of China; and                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Royalty shall be paid in accordance with relevant regulations of the People's Republic                 <br /><br /><br />
of China.                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
13.2.2    The Annual Gross Production of Crude Oil shall, after payment for Value Added Tax                   <br /><br /><br />
and Royalty in accordance with Article 13.2.1 herein, be firstly deemed as the “cost recovery oil” and        <br /><br /><br />
shall be used for payment or for cost recovery in the following sequence:                                     <br /><br /><br />
13.2.2.1 Payment in kind for the Operating Costs actually incurred but not yet recovered by                   <br /><br /><br />
the Parties pursuant to Article 12.1.3 hereof after the price of the said “cost recovery oil” has been        <br /><br /><br />
determined in accordance with Article 14 hereof.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
13.2.2.2 The remainder of the “cost recovery oil” shall after payment for Operating Costs in                  <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Article 13.2.2.1 herein be deemed as “investment recovery oil”. Such “investment              <br /><br /><br />
recovery oil” pursuant to the Crude Oil price determined in accordance with Article 14 shall be used          <br /><br /><br />
for the simultaneous recovery of the Pilot Test Costs and the Development Costs incurred by the               <br /><br /><br />
Contractor in accordance with Articles 12.1.1 and 12.1.2 and the Pre-development Costs spent by               <br /><br /><br />
CNPC as stipulated in Article 12.3 in proportion of eighty-two percent (82%) by the Contractor and            <br /><br /><br />
eighteen percent (18%) by CNPC. The unrecovered costs of the Parties shall be carried forward to              <br /><br /><br />
and recovered from the “investment recovery oil” in succeeding Calendar Years until fully recovered.          <br /><br /><br />
The date that the said Pilot Test Costs and Development Costs have been recovered by the Contractor           <br /><br /><br />
shall be deemed as the date that the investment recovery period has ended. By the date of expiration          <br /><br /><br />
of the production period pursuant to Article 4.5 hereof, if the said costs incurred by the Parties have       <br /><br /><br />
not been fully recovered, then such unrecovered costs shall be regarded as a loss and the Parties shall       <br /><br /><br />
respectively bear the loss.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
13.2.3 At the end of the investment recovery period, the remainder of the Annual Gross                        <br /><br /><br />
Production of Crude Oil after the allocation referred to in Articles 13.2.1 and 13.2.2 herein                 <br /><br /><br />
(hereinafter referred to as “allocable remainder oil”) shall be allocated in proportion of CNPC fifty-        <br /><br /><br />
one percent (51%), the Contractor forty-nine percent (49%).                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                            33                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿13.3    CNPC and each company comprising the Contractor shall, throughout the entire                          <br /><br /><br />
Contract Term, have the right and obligation in each Calendar Quarter, to lift and take, and separately       <br /><br /><br />
dispose of their respective full shares of all Crude Oil produced, and determined pursuant to Articles        <br /><br /><br />
13.2.2 and 13.2.3 herein.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
In the event that the Crude Oil production of the Oil Field is reduced because CNPC or any                    <br /><br /><br />
company comprising the Contractor does not lift and take its full share of Crude Oil or lifts nothing,        <br /><br /><br />
then, such reduction in Crude Oil production shall not affect the total amount of Crude Oil due to each       <br /><br /><br />
of the other Parties or the amounts of Crude Oil available to be lifted and disposed by each of the           <br /><br /><br />
other Parties as provided in Article 13.4 (c) herein.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
13.4    A Crude Oil lifting procedure shall be agreed upon by the Parties no later than six (6)               <br /><br /><br />
months prior to the Date of Commencement of Commercial Production of the Oil Field within the                 <br /><br /><br />
Contract Area and shall include, but not be limited to:                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(a)    the Operator's notification of Crude Oil production to CNPC and each company                           <br /><br /><br />
comprising the Contractor;                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(b)    notification by CNPC and each company comprising the Contractor of its expected                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
offtake to the Operator;                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(c)    the Operator's notification to CNPC and each company comprising the Contractor of                      <br /><br /><br />
the final Crude Oil lifting schedule prepared by the Crude Oil lifting coordination group in accordance       <br /><br /><br />
with Article 13.5 herein, which shall be binding on CNPC and each company comprising the                      <br /><br /><br />
Contractor;                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(d)    limitation and calculation of overlift and underlift of CNPC and each company                          <br /><br /><br />
comprising the Contractor; and provisions to ensure timely and ratable lifting of Crude Oil;                  <br /><br /><br />
(e)    determination of allowable operational tolerance on lifting; and                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(f)    other terminal procedures as may be required to reflect the particular circumstances.                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
13.5 For the purpose of implementing the procedures as described in Article 13.4 herein,                      <br /><br /><br />
CNPC and each company comprising the Contractor shall jointly set up a Crude Oil lifting                      <br /><br /><br />
coordination group consisting of representatives, one each appointed by CNPC and each company                 <br /><br /><br />
comprising the Contractor, with the representative of CNPC as the chairman, and one representative            <br /><br /><br />
of the Contractor or each company comprising the Contractor as the vice chairman. Such group shall            <br /><br /><br />
be responsible for the preparation of Crude Oil lifting plans for each Calendar Year, for Calendar            <br /><br /><br />
Quarter and for calendar month and shall also be responsible for the reasonable and unified                   <br /><br /><br />
arrangements and adjustments of the aforesaid Crude Oil lifting plans through close contact with any          <br /><br /><br />
operator in charge of the storage and loading facilities.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
13.6 The Contractor shall have the right to export from China all Crude Oil which it                          <br /><br /><br />
obtains as set forth in Article 13.2.2 and 13.2.3 herein. The Contractor shall obtain, with the               <br /><br /><br />
assistance of CNPC, any export license or other permit that may be required in order for the                  <br /><br /><br />
Contractor to export from China all Crude Oil which it obtains as set forth in Article 13.2.2 and 13.2.3      <br /><br /><br />
herein.                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <5 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />

﻿13.7 At the expiration of the pilot test period, if the Contractor opts to terminate the                <br /><br /><br />
Contract, the amount of Crude Oil extracted from the Oil Field during the pilot test period shall be    <br /><br /><br />
allocated in proportion of CNPC sixty percent (60%), the Contractor forty percent (40%); if the         <br /><br /><br />
Contractor opts to enter into the development period, the amount of Crude Oil extracted from the Oil    <br /><br /><br />
Field during the pilot test period shall be allocated in accordance with Article 13.2.2.2 herein. The   <br /><br /><br />
amount of Crude Oil extracted from the Oil Field within the Contract Area from the date of the          <br /><br /><br />
approval of the Overall Development Program to the Date of Commencement of Commercial                   <br /><br /><br />
Production shall be allocated in accordance with Article 13.2.2.2 herein.                               <br /><br /><br />
