 35                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                              Article 14                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                  Quality, Quantity, Price and Destination of Crude Oil                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
14.1    Quality of the Crude Oil                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
14.1.1    The quality analysis of Crude Oil produced from the Oil Field within the Contract                   <br /><br /><br />
Area shall be undertaken at the Delivery Point. Such analysis shall be carried out on a sample taken          <br /><br /><br />
by the State Bureau of Import and Export Commodities Inspection (hereafter referred to as the                 <br /><br /><br />
“Bureau”) or any representative agency authorized by the Bureau pursuant to standards issued by the           <br /><br /><br />
State Bureau of Standardization of the People's Republic of China or by the Department or Unit.               <br /><br /><br />
14.1.2    The Crude Oil quality analysis referred to in Article 14.1.1 above shall include the                <br /><br /><br />
following:                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(a)    density at 20 degree centigrade, in grams per cubic centimeter;                                        <br /><br /><br />
(b)    sulfur content, in weight percentage;                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(c)    water content, in weight percentage; and                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(d)    basic sediment content, in weight percentage                                                           <br /><br /><br />
14.2    Quantity of the Crude Oil                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
14.2.1    The quantity measurement of the Crude Oil produced from the Oil Field within the                    <br /><br /><br />
Contract Area, when being lifted, shall be made at a Delivery Point and with measuring devices both           <br /><br /><br />
to be agreed upon by the Parties. A relevant measuring organization of the Chinese Government or a            <br /><br /><br />
representative agency authorized thereby shall, at appropriate regular intervals, calibrate all the           <br /><br /><br />
measuring devices, conduct special testing and issue certificates of qualification with respect thereto       <br /><br /><br />
or confirm their qualification before the measuring devices are put into use. The quality and quantity        <br /><br /><br />
of the Crude Oil delivered shall be authenticated in accordance with the commodity quality certificate        <br /><br /><br />
and weight certificate issued by the Bureau and such quality and quantity shall be the basis for the          <br /><br /><br />
accounting settlement.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
14.2.2    If any Party to the Contract believes that the Crude Oil measuring devices, sampling                <br /><br /><br />
or analysis are inaccurate, or has any objection to the results specified in the above mentioned              <br /><br /><br />
certificates, on-site investigations, technical exchanges and discussions may be conducted by the             <br /><br /><br />
Parties to resolve the issue in a manner satisfactory to the Parties.                                         <br /><br /><br />
14.3 Determination of the Crude Oil Price                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
14.3.1 The price of various grades of the Crude Oil shall be expressed as a FOB price at the                  <br /><br /><br />
Delivery Point. Determination of the Crude Oil price shall be made with reference to the prevailing           <br /><br /><br />
price in arm's length transactions of similar quality Crude Oil on the main world oil markets and the         <br /><br /><br />
adjustment in such price shall be made in accordance with such determinants as the quality of the             <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oil, the terms of delivery, transportation and payment and other terms.                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                            36                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿The aforesaid price in arm's length transactions in this Article refers to a price at which a                 <br /><br /><br />
seller sells its crude oil to a buyer who is independent of the seller, but not including the prices used     <br /><br /><br />
by them for government to government transactions which do not reflect international oil market               <br /><br /><br />
price, Crude Oil exchange, or barter transactions.                                                            <br /><br /><br />
14.3.2    Subject to the agreement of Parties, where the Crude Oil produced from the Oil Field                <br /><br /><br />
within the Contract Area differs in grades, the prices of such Crude Oil with different quality will be       <br /><br /><br />
individually determined.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
14.3.3    The price of the Crude Oil produced from the Oil Field within the Contract Area shall               <br /><br /><br />
be denominated in U.S. Dollars per metric ton. However, if an international currency other than the           <br /><br /><br />
U.S. Dollar prevails on the main world oil markets as the pricing unit of Crude Oil, the Parties may          <br /><br /><br />
also use that international currency therefore upon mutual agreement.                                         <br /><br /><br />
14.3.4    Procedure for the Determination of the Crude Oil Price                                              <br /><br /><br />
14.3.4.1    The Crude Oil price shall be determined once each Calendar Quarter. In case                       <br /><br /><br />
the Crude Oil price prevailing on most world oil markets fluctuates, CNPC and the Contractor each             <br /><br /><br />
shall have the right to propose, at any time, that a new Crude Oil price be negotiated and determined.        <br /><br /><br />
14.3.4.2    The Contractor shall, no later than forty-five (45) days prior to the                             <br /><br /><br />
commencement of any Calendar Quarter, notify CNPC of its proposed price for Crude Oil to be lifted            <br /><br /><br />
in such Calendar Quarter (for the purpose of this Article hereafter referred to as the said Calendar          <br /><br /><br />
Quarter).                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
14.3.4.3    CNPC shall notify the Contractor of its decided price within ten (10) days                        <br /><br /><br />
after the receipt of the aforesaid proposed price notified by the Contractor. In the absence of a             <br /><br /><br />
different price notified by CNPC to the Contractor within ten (10) days after the receipt of the              <br /><br /><br />
aforesaid notification, the proposed price notified by the Contractor as referred to in Article 14.3.4.2      <br /><br /><br />
herein shall be applied to the Crude Oil to be lifted in the said Calendar Quarter.                           <br /><br /><br />
14.3.4.4    The Contractor shall, within five (5) days following its receipt of notice of a                   <br /><br /><br />
price decided by CNPC, state to CNPC whether the price is acceptable. If it is acceptable, then the           <br /><br /><br />
said decided price shall be regarded as the price agreed upon by the Parties for the said Calendar            <br /><br /><br />
Quarter. If it is not acceptable, the Parties shall, within ten (10) days, carry out further negotiation in   <br /><br /><br />
an amicable manner to determine the price for the said Calendar Quarter.                                      <br /><br /><br />
14.3.4.5    In the event that the Parties still cannot reach an agreement on the Crude Oil                    <br /><br /><br />
price for the said Calendar Quarter through further negotiations by the Parties, the Contractor may lift      <br /><br /><br />
the Crude Oil in accordance with the quota specified for the said Calendar Quarter in Article 13.2            <br /><br /><br />
hereof, and the Crude Oil price for the preceding Calendar Quarter shall apply provisionally to the           <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oil of such quota and the payment shall be made accordingly. Then, the Parties shall negotiate          <br /><br /><br />
further on the Crude Oil price for the said Calendar Quarter, taking into account relevant independent        <br /><br /><br />
and non-proprietary market data on Third Party sales of Crude Oil in substantial quantities on the            <br /><br /><br />
main world oil markets, adjusted for quality, transportation and other applicable differentials. The          <br /><br /><br />
Parties shall each take into account the information supplied and discussed and attempt to agree on a         <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oil price based upon such information by the end of the said Calendar Quarter.                          <br /><br /><br />
(1) In the event that the Parties still cannot reach an agreement in Crude Oil price by the                   <br /><br /><br />
end of the said Calendar Quarter, then the Crude Oil price shall be the weighted average FOB price of         <br /><br /><br />
the Crude Oil of the same or similar quality sold by CNPC and/or the Contractor to a Third Party or           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 37                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿Third Parties and produced in the said Calendar Quarter from the Oil Fields described hereafter,               <br /><br /><br />
adjusted for such differences as the quality, delivery, transportation, payment and other terms, but           <br /><br /><br />
excluding the government to government transactions which do not reflect international oil market              <br /><br /><br />
price, Crude Oil exchange, barter or spot transactions.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
The application of the above-mentioned price of Crude Oil sold to a Third Party or Third                       <br /><br /><br />
Parties shall be in the following sequence:                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(i)    Firstly, the price, calculated and determined in accordance with the above mentioned                    <br /><br /><br />
stipulations, of the Crude Oil produced from the relevant Oil Field or Oil Fields in the Contract Area         <br /><br /><br />
and sold to a Third Party or Third Parties shall be applied;                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(ii)    In the event no sales as referred to in paragraph (i) above were made in the said                      <br /><br /><br />
Calendar Quarter, the price, calculated and determined in accordance with the above mentioned                  <br /><br /><br />
stipulations, of the Crude Oil produced from other Oil Field in the Contract Area and sold to a Third          <br /><br /><br />
Party or Third Parties shall be applied; and                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(iii)    In the event no sales mentioned in paragraphs (i) and (ii) above were made in the said                <br /><br /><br />
Calendar Quarter, the price, calculated and determined in accordance with the above-mentioned                  <br /><br /><br />
stipulations, of the Crude Oil produced from the Oil Fields of other contract areas for Chinese-foreign        <br /><br /><br />
cooperative exploitation of Petroleum resources and sold to a Third Party or Third Parties shall be            <br /><br /><br />
applied;                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(2)    In the event there are no such Third Party sales of the Crude Oil as referred to in Article             <br /><br /><br />
14.3.4.5(1) herein during the said Calendar Quarter, then the Crude Oil price for the said Calendar            <br /><br /><br />
Quarter shall be equal to the same Crude Oil price of the preceding Calendar Quarter adjusted by the           <br /><br /><br />
differences in the arithmetic average of the average daily selling price for a basket of three or more         <br /><br /><br />
internationally traded Crude Oils in the said Calendar Quarter compared with that for such basket of           <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oils for the preceding Calendar Quarter. The adjusted price shall be the Crude Oil price for the         <br /><br /><br />
said Calendar Quarter. The Crude Oils selected for the basket shall each be similar in quality to the          <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oil from the Contract Area and chosen from different countries and shall have prices which               <br /><br /><br />
reflect the conditions of the main world oil markets and shall be mutually agreed by the Parties in the        <br /><br /><br />
Overall Development Program. Any Crude Oil selected for the basket may be substituted at any time              <br /><br /><br />
by another Crude Oil upon agreement by the Parties.                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(3)    If the Parties are unable to agree on a Crude Oil price for a Calendar Quarter in which                 <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oil is first produced and delivered from or the production of Crude Oil is restored in the Oil           <br /><br /><br />
Field in the Contract Area, then the Crude Oil for the Calendar Quarter shall be priced and/or paid in         <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the arithmetic average price of the prices finally proposed by the Parties in the              <br /><br /><br />
Calendar Quarter. Based on the Crude Oil price agreed upon by the Parties for the succeeding                   <br /><br /><br />
Calendar Quarter, the Crude Oil price for the Calendar Quarter shall be determined by adjusting                <br /><br /><br />
retroactively by the difference between the arithmetic average prices of the basket of the Crude Oils          <br /><br /><br />
for the Calendar Quarter and the succeeding Calendar Quarter in accordance with the calculation                <br /><br /><br />
method referred to in Article 14.3.4.5(2) herein.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
14.3.4.6    If, due to the delayed announcement of crude oil prices by the main world                          <br /><br /><br />
oil-producing countries or the main world oil markets, or if, as agreed by CNPC and the Contractor,            <br /><br /><br />
an unstable main world oil market exists, then, the period for the determination of the price referred to      <br /><br /><br />
in Article 14.3.4.2 herein may be extended to the end of the said Calendar Quarter in question.                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            rf <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 38                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿14.3.4.7 If the Crude Oil prices in the international oil markets or the Crude Oil prices               <br /><br /><br />
quoted in the main oil-producing countries change materially, then the Parties wiU meet and agree to    <br /><br /><br />
adjust the Crude Oil price retroactively. The period for such retroactive adjustment shall not exceed   <br /><br /><br />
the previous Calendar Quarter.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
14.3.5    The Crude Oil for each Calendar Quarter due to CNPC pursuant to Article 13 hereof             <br /><br /><br />
shall be converted into an amount of money in the currency utilized pursuant to Article 14.3.3 herein   <br /><br /><br />
based on the Crude Oil price for that Calendar Quarter finally determined in accordance with the        <br /><br /><br />
aforesaid provisions specified in Article 14.3 herein and such amount of money shall be entered into    <br /><br /><br />
the Joint Account as of the date on which such Crude Oil is lifted.                                     <br /><br /><br />
14.3.6    The Crude Oil for each Calendar Quarter due to the Contractor pursuant to Article 13          <br /><br /><br />
hereof shall be converted into an amount of money in the currency utilized pursuant to Article 14.3.3   <br /><br /><br />
herein based on the Crude Oil price for that Calendar Quarter finally determined in accordance with     <br /><br /><br />
the aforesaid provisions specified in Article 14.3 herein and such amount of money shall be entered     <br /><br /><br />
into the Joint Account as of the date on which the Crude Oil is lifted.                                 <br /><br /><br />
14.4 Destination of the Crude Oil                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
14.4.1    The destination of Contractor's Crude Oil obtained under the Contract shall be at the         <br /><br /><br />
discretion of the Contractor, except as stipulated in Article 14.4.2 herein.                            <br /><br /><br />
14.4.2    In accordance with the decisions of the Chinese Government, CNPC shall notify the             <br /><br /><br />
Contractor of any prohibited destinations, which infringe on the political interests of the People's    <br /><br /><br />
Republic of China. The Contractor shall not deliver the Crude Oil to the prohibited destinations as     <br /><br /><br />
notified.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 39                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                          Article 15                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                          Preference to the Employment of the                                                <br /><br /><br />
                         Chinese Personnel, Goods and Services                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
15.1    For the performance of the Petroleum Operations, the Contractor's procurement of                     <br /><br /><br />
necessary goods, leasing equipment and signature of subcontracts or other service contracts shall be         <br /><br /><br />
subject to Article 22 of the Petroleum Regulations. The Contractor shall give preference to Chinese          <br /><br /><br />
goods, equipment and service provided that they are competitive in terms of price, quality and term of       <br /><br /><br />
delivery.                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
15.2    The Contractor shall give preference to the employment of Chinese Personnel in the                   <br /><br /><br />
performance of the Petroleum Operations in accordance with Article 18 of the Petroleum Regulations.          <br /><br /><br />
For this purpose, the Contractor shall submit in advance to CNPC and JMC respectively a plan for the         <br /><br /><br />
employment of Chinese Personnel listing all the posts and number of the persons involved. CNPC               <br /><br /><br />
shall, in accordance with the plan, provide or assist in recruiting Chinese employee candidates for          <br /><br /><br />
such employment. For the performance of Petroleum Operations, the Contractor shall have the                  <br /><br /><br />
obligation to employ competent Chinese Personnel and to employ those who have become qualified               <br /><br /><br />
after being trained in accordance with the training program. The Contractor shall give preference in         <br /><br /><br />
employing the Chinese Personnel who have participated in the training program provided by the                <br /><br /><br />
Contractor.                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
15.3    The engineering design corporations under or entrusted by CNPC shall have the right                  <br /><br /><br />
to participate in the master designs and engineering designs made by the Contractor for the purpose of       <br /><br /><br />
the implementation of the Contract. Engineering design companies within the territory of the People's        <br /><br /><br />
Republic of China shall be given preference in entering into the subcontracts for the aforesaid master       <br /><br /><br />
designs and engineering designs, provided that their technical level, quality, price and delivery time       <br /><br /><br />
are competitive.                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
15.4    After the Contractor signs equipment leasing contracts, service contracts or                         <br /><br /><br />
subcontracts with CNPC or its Affiliates in accordance with Article 15.1 herein, the Contractor shall        <br /><br /><br />
endeavor to provide technical assistance to CNPC or its Affiliates, at the request of CNPC, so as to         <br /><br /><br />
enable them to meet the needs of operations to be undertaken. The expenses so incurred shall be borne        <br /><br /><br />
by CNPC or its Affiliates.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                       40                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                Article 16                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                               Training of Chinese Personnel                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                 and Transfer of Technology                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
16.1    Contractor agrees, in the course of the Petroleum Operations, to transfer to CNPC and                   <br /><br /><br />
its Affiliates, the advanced technology and managerial experience including patented technology,                <br /><br /><br />
know-how or other confidential technology, etc. used in the performance of the Petroleum Operations             <br /><br /><br />
and the necessary data and/or information for mastering such technology and experience in                       <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Article 18 of the Petroleum Regulations, provided, however, such technology to be               <br /><br /><br />
transferred shall be proprietary to the Contractor and if the transfer of any of such technology is             <br /><br /><br />
restricted in any way during the term of the Contract, the Contractor shall, to the extent reasonably           <br /><br /><br />
possible, endeavor to obtain permission for the transfer of such restricted technology. The Contractor          <br /><br /><br />
agrees to train the Chinese Personnel including workers, technical, economic, managerial, legal and             <br /><br /><br />
other professional personnel, in order to improve their technical and/or managerial capabilities.               <br /><br /><br />
Details of training of Chinese Personnel and transfer of technology are described in Annex IV -                 <br /><br /><br />
Training of Chinese Personnel and Transfer of Technology hereto.                                                <br /><br /><br />
16.2    Within ninety (90) days following the Date of Commencement of the Implementation                        <br /><br /><br />
of the Contract, the Contractor shall, after consultation with CNPC, complete and submit a training             <br /><br /><br />
and technology transfer program for the Chinese Personnel in the pilot test period and the                      <br /><br /><br />
corresponding budget to JMC for review and approval, and upon approval by JMC, put it into                      <br /><br /><br />
practice. The Contractor shall, after consultation with CNPC, complete and submit training and                  <br /><br /><br />
technology transfer programs and corresponding budgets for the Chinese Personnel in the                         <br /><br /><br />
development period and the production period, respectively, to JMC for its review and approval                  <br /><br /><br />
before the commencement of the Production Operations, and upon approval by JMC, put them into                   <br /><br /><br />
practice in time so as to have ample time in advance for such training and technology transfer.                 <br /><br /><br />
16.3    The purpose, requirement, fields of specialization, scope of personnel, specific job                    <br /><br /><br />
categories, type, method, etc. in respect of training of Chinese Personnel and transfer of technology           <br /><br /><br />
shall be determined in Annex IV -Training of Chinese Personnel and Transfer of Technology hereto.               <br /><br /><br />
16.4    The expenses and costs incurred for performing the training and technology transfer                     <br /><br /><br />
program stipulated in this Article shall be borne by the Contractor.                                            <br /><br /><br />
16.5    In the course of the implementation of the Contract, the Parties shall have scientific                  <br /><br /><br />
and technical cooperation and academic exchange in connection with the Petroleum Operations. The                <br /><br /><br />
relevant provisions concerning the plan, participating personnel and type related to the scientific and         <br /><br /><br />
technical cooperation and academic exchange shall be determined by the Parties. The expenses                    <br /><br /><br />
required by the scientific and technical cooperation and academic exchange shall be included in the             <br /><br /><br />
budget specified in Article 16.2 herein and charged to the Joint Account. All inventions, experiments           <br /><br /><br />
or research results arising from the said cooperation and academic exchange shall be shared by and              <br /><br /><br />
belong to the Parties who, subject to the provisions of Article 22 hereof, shall not disclose them to any       <br /><br /><br />
Third Party.                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
16.5.1 In the course of the implementation of the Contract, those scientific research projects                  <br /><br /><br />
which are required by the Petroleum Operations but not carried out by the Parties may, with the                 <br /><br /><br />
approval of JMC, be commissioned to, and carried out by, any Third Party. The Operator shall enter              <br /><br /><br />
into subcontracts or service contracts with relevant scientific research departments within the territory       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                              41                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿of the People's Republic of China, provided that they are competent and competitive. The aforesaid           <br /><br /><br />
required expenses shall be included in the budget specified in Article 16.2 herein and charged to the        <br /><br /><br />
Joint Account. All inventions and experimental or research results developed from the aforesaid              <br /><br /><br />
research projects carried out by a Third Party delegated by the Operator shall also be shared by and         <br /><br /><br />
belong to the Parties who, subject to the provisions of Article 22 hereof, shall not disclose any of them    <br /><br /><br />
to any other Third Parties. The Operator shall endeavor to incorporate the provisions herein in the          <br /><br /><br />
subcontracts or service contracts signed with a Third Party.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
16.6 The advanced technology and managerial experience, including patented technology,                       <br /><br /><br />
know-how or other confidential technology that the Contractor transfers to CNPC, shall remain the            <br /><br /><br />
exclusive property of the Contractor and also be subject to the confidentiality restrictions of Article 22   <br /><br /><br />
hereof.                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
16.7 For the purpose of the implementation of Article 16 herein and Annex TV-Training of                     <br /><br /><br />
Chinese Personnel and Transfer of Technology hereto, the costs and expenditures incurred by the              <br /><br /><br />
Contractor annually for training of Chinese Personnel and transfer of technology shall be: Seventy-          <br /><br /><br />
five Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$75,000) per year during the pilot test period; Two Hundred                    <br /><br /><br />
Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$200,000) per year during the development period; One Hundred and                   <br /><br /><br />
Sixty-five Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$165,000) per year for the first fifteen (15) years of the               <br /><br /><br />
production period and One Hundred Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$100,000) per year for years sixteen              <br /><br /><br />
(16) to twenty (20) of the production period.                                                                <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                             Article 17                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                              Ownership of Assets and Data                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
17.1    All assets purchased, installed and constructed under the Work Program and budget                    <br /><br /><br />
for the Oil Field within the Contract Area shall be owned by CNPC from the date on which the                 <br /><br /><br />
production period expires or if the Contractor opts to terminate the Contract at the expiration of the       <br /><br /><br />
pilot test period, from the date on which the pilot test period expires. The Operator shall be               <br /><br /><br />
responsible for the acceptance inspection or testing of the said assets and CNPC may, as it deems            <br /><br /><br />
necessary, send its experts to participate in such acceptance inspection or testing. Such assets shall       <br /><br /><br />
not be used in any operations other than the Petroleum Operations or any operations by Third Parties         <br /><br /><br />
without the,consent of the Parties.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
17.2    Equipment and facilities which are owned by a Third Party and are either leased by                   <br /><br /><br />
the Operator or temporarily brought into the territory of the People's Republic of China for the             <br /><br /><br />
performance of the Petroleum Operations shall not be deemed as assets owned by CNPC. Such                    <br /><br /><br />
equipment and facilities may be exported from the People's Republic of China, and CNPC shall assist          <br /><br /><br />
in handling export formalities.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
17.3    The ownership of all of the data, records, samples, vouchers, and other original data                <br /><br /><br />
obtained in the course of performing the Petroleum Operations shall vest in CNPC. For the purpose            <br /><br /><br />
of implementation of the Contract, the availability and sale of all the data related to the Contract         <br /><br /><br />
owned by CNPC required by the Contractor shall be made through CNPC.                                         <br /><br /><br />

                                           43                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                Article 18                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                   Associated Natural Gas                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
18.1    Associated Natural Gas                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
18.1.1    The Associated Natural Gas produced from the Oil Field within the Contract                            <br /><br /><br />
Area shall be primarily used for purposes related to the operations of production and production                <br /><br /><br />
enhancement of Oil Fields such as gas injection, gas lifting, steam and heat generation and power               <br /><br /><br />
generation.                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
18.1.2    Based on the principle of full utilization of the Associated Natural Gas and                          <br /><br /><br />
with no impediment to normal production of the Crude Oil, the Overall Development Program of the                <br /><br /><br />
Oil Field shall include a plan of utilization of the Associated Natural Gas. If there is any excess             <br /><br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas in the Oil Field after utilization pursuant to Article 18.1.1 herein (hereafter          <br /><br /><br />
referred to as “excess Associated Natural Gas”), the Operator shall carry out a feasibility study               <br /><br /><br />
regarding the utilization of such excess Associated Natural Gas of such Oil Field. Such feasibility             <br /><br /><br />
study, if carried out before the Development Operations of the Oil Field, shall be included as part of          <br /><br /><br />
the feasibility study on the development of the Oil Field. With respect to the Oil Field already under          <br /><br /><br />
commercial production, if a further feasibility study on the utilization of its excess Associated Natural       <br /><br /><br />
Gas is required, such study shall be carried out by the Operator and a report thereon shall be submitted        <br /><br /><br />
to JMC for review and discussion. If the Parties decide to utilize the excess Associated Natural Gas            <br /><br /><br />
of the Oil Field, the construction of facilities for such utilization and the production of the excess          <br /><br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas shall be carried out at the same time as the Oil Field construction and                  <br /><br /><br />
production.                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
18.1.2.1    If the Parties agree that the excess Associated Natural Gas of the Oil Field                        <br /><br /><br />
has no commercial value, then such gas shall be disposed of by the Operator subject to relevant                 <br /><br /><br />
regulations concerning the environmental protection, provided that there is no impediment to normal             <br /><br /><br />
production of the Crude Oil.                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
18.1.2.2    If any Party to the Contract considers unilaterally that the excess Associated                      <br /><br /><br />
Natural Gas of the Oil Field has commercial value, such gas may be utilized by that Party at its own            <br /><br /><br />
expense without affecting timing and optimal development of the Oil Field concerned, the amount of              <br /><br /><br />
“cost recovery oil” and “allocable remainder oil” due to the other Party to the Contract which does not         <br /><br /><br />
invest in such utilization.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
18.1.2.3    If the Parties agree that excess Associated Natural Gas of the Oil Field has                        <br /><br /><br />
commercial value, the Contractor shall make further investment in its utilization, and the aforesaid            <br /><br /><br />
new investment shall not affect either the proportion of “cost recovery oil” by the Parties stipulated in       <br /><br /><br />
Article 13.2.2 hereof or the proportion of the “allocable remainder oil” by the Parties stipulated in           <br /><br /><br />
Article 13.2.3 hereof. If the Parties disagree on the commercial utilization of such excess Associated          <br /><br /><br />
Natural Gas of that Oil Field, they shall, guided by the principle of mutual benefit, carry out further         <br /><br /><br />
negotiations to reach an agreement in writing.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
If the Parties fail to reach agreement through negotiations, CNPC shall reserve the right to                    <br /><br /><br />
dispose of the excess Associated Natural Gas of the said Oil Field unilaterally. If CNPC decides to             <br /><br /><br />
utilize the said excess Associated Natural Gas, the Contractor shall have the right to join in the              <br /><br /><br />
utilization of the said excess Associated Natural Gas within three (3) years after the facilities for           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                              44                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿utilizing the said excess Associated Natural Gas are completed unilaterally by CNPC in accordance             <br /><br /><br />
with an Associated Natural Gas utilization program formulated by CNPC. If the Contractor decides in           <br /><br /><br />
writing to participate in the utilization of the said excess Associated Natural Gas within the three (3)      <br /><br /><br />
years mentioned above, then, the Contractor shall pay CNPC an amount of money, in addition to the             <br /><br /><br />
cost spent by CNPC on the said utilization of excess Associated Natural Gas up to the date of                 <br /><br /><br />
Contractor's submission of the written notice to CNPC. Such amount shall be equal to two times                <br /><br /><br />
(200%) of the foregoing costs for utilization of the excess Associated Natural Gas and such amount of         <br /><br /><br />
money shall not be charged into the Joint Account. Thereafter, the costs to be: incurred in such              <br /><br /><br />
utilization of excess Associated Natural Gas shall be provided by the Contractor solely in accordance         <br /><br /><br />
with the provisions herein.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
If the Contractor decides, after the three (3) years mentioned above, not to participate in the               <br /><br /><br />
utilization of the excess Associated Natural Gas, the Contractor shall be deemed to have waived all its       <br /><br /><br />
rights to use the said excess Associated Natural Gas.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
18.1.3    Expenses incurred in the utilization of the Associated Natural Gas of the Oil                       <br /><br /><br />
Field as stipulated in Article 18.1.1 herein, and those incurred in carrying out a feasibility study on the   <br /><br /><br />
utilization of the excess Associated Natural Gas after commencement of commercial production of the           <br /><br /><br />
Oil Field referred to in Article 18.1.2 herein shall be charged to the Development Costs of the Oil           <br /><br /><br />
Field.                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
Royalty and Value Added Tax of the production of the excess Associated Natural Gas shall                      <br /><br /><br />
be paid to die Chinese Government through CNPC.                                                               <br /><br /><br />
All remaining excess Associated Natural Gas after the deduction of Value Added Tax and                        <br /><br /><br />
Royalty shall be allocated to CNPC and the Contractor by analogy in accordance with the proportion            <br /><br /><br />
stipulated in Article 13 herein.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
18.2 If CNPC unilaterally utilizes the excess Associated Natural Gas of the Oil Field and                     <br /><br /><br />
requires to apply the Contractor's appropriate and advanced technology and managerial experience,             <br /><br /><br />
the Parties shall negotiate terms and conditions related thereto and the Operator shall carry out the         <br /><br /><br />
operations if an agreement is reached on such terms and conditions.                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 45                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                       Article 19                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                      Accounting, Auditing and Personnel Costs                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
19.1    Accounting                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
Annex II - Accounting Procedure hereto contains the guidelines for the Operator to keep                       <br /><br /><br />
accounting books and records and make financial settlements. The Operator shall keep and settle the           <br /><br /><br />
accounts for all the financial activities in respect of the Contract Area and maintain all the accounting     <br /><br /><br />
books and records in accordance with Annex II - Accounting Procedure hereto in order to accurately            <br /><br /><br />
reflect the Pilot Test Costs and the Development Costs thereon and Operating Costs incurred in the            <br /><br /><br />
performance of the Petroleum Operations in respect of the Contract Area, as wrell as quantity and             <br /><br /><br />
monetary value of the production and allocation of Crude Oil and Natural Gas. The Operator shall              <br /><br /><br />
submit detailed statements and relevant written reports to JMC and the departments concerned.                 <br /><br /><br />
19.2    Auditing                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
19.2.1    Any Party to the Contract shall have the right to audit all the Operator's Joint                    <br /><br /><br />
Account accounting books and records after the end of each Calendar Year and give die Operator a              <br /><br /><br />
written notice of the auditing results. The auditing shall be completed within twenty-four (24) months        <br /><br /><br />
after the end of each Calendar Year. In the absence of any written notice of the exception to the             <br /><br /><br />
auditing results given by such Party within such period or if the annual Joint Account accounting             <br /><br /><br />
books and records of the Operator are not audited by any non-Operator Party within such period, the           <br /><br /><br />
Operator's Joint Account accounting books and records shall be deemed correct A special auditing of           <br /><br /><br />
the Operator's Joint Account accounting books and records may be made due to some special                     <br /><br /><br />
requirements during a Calendar Year.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
19.2.2    If the auditing referred to in Article 19.2.1 herein is conducted, the Operator                     <br /><br /><br />
shall be given thirty (30) days' notice prior to the date of commencement of such awiiting. There shall       <br /><br /><br />
be no impediment to normal Petroleum Operations during the period of any audit.                               <br /><br /><br />
19.2.3    The auditors shall be entitled to access to all relevant Joint Account records,                     <br /><br /><br />
files and other information and may inspect such sites and facilities as necessary.                           <br /><br /><br />
19.2.4    Upon receipt of a notice of any Party’s exceptions to the auditing results, the                     <br /><br /><br />
Operator shall resolve these matters in due time (no later than sixty (60) days thereafter).                  <br /><br /><br />
19.3 Personnel Costs                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
19.3.1    The personnel costs mean the remuneration and other related charges paid on                         <br /><br /><br />
the basis of the working time spent by personnel who are engaged in administration, management,               <br /><br /><br />
accounting, finance, tax, employee relations, procurement, legal affairs, computer services,                  <br /><br /><br />
engineering, geology, geophysics, drilling and Production Operations as well as all other work for the        <br /><br /><br />
implementation of the Contract.                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
19.3.1.1    The salaries or wages of personnel in various subordinate bodies of JMC and                       <br /><br /><br />
of all employees engaged in the performance of the Petroleum Operations shall be included in the              <br /><br /><br />
personnel costs as provided in Article 19.3.1 herein.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
﻿19.3.1.2    Personnel costs which are classified as the overhead of the superior                       <br /><br /><br />
management organization pursuant to Article 5.2.18 of Annex II - Accounting Procedure hereto shall     <br /><br /><br />
not be included in the personnel costs mentioned herein.                                               <br /><br /><br />
19.3.2    After the Date of Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract, the                    <br /><br /><br />
Operator shall work out a staffing plan for its organization and a personnel costs plan with respect   <br /><br /><br />
thereto (including an itemized plan of personnel costs, such as basic salary or wage, overseas         <br /><br /><br />
allowance and area allowance, etc.) before the beginning of each Calendar Year and submit such plan    <br /><br /><br />
with the annual Work Program and budget to JMC for review and approval.                                <br /><br /><br />
The Contractor shall provide CNPC with itemized information of personnel costs of the                  <br /><br /><br />
Expatriate Employees. CNPC shall bear the obligation of confidentiality to such information            <br /><br /><br />
provided by the Contractor.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
The Operator shall charge the personnel costs of the Contractor’s personnel actually incurred          <br /><br /><br />
to the Joint Account. CNPC shall have the right to audit the personnel costs charged to the Joint      <br /><br /><br />
Account.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
19.3.3    The settlement of all charges for the salaries and wages of CNPC personnel                   <br /><br /><br />
mentioned in the second paragraph of Article 7.7 hereof shall be made between CNPC and the             <br /><br /><br />
Operator, and CNPC personnel shall be responsible for all individual income tax in accordance with     <br /><br /><br />
the provisions of the individual income tax law of the People's Republic of China.                     <br /><br /><br />
19.3.4    In the pilot test period and the development period, the level of the salaries               <br /><br /><br />
and wages and other related charges paid to the Expatriate Employees shall be made by the Contractor   <br /><br /><br />
through consultation with CNPC. After the Date of Commencement of Commercial Production of the         <br /><br /><br />
Oil Field, the level of the salaries and wages and other related charges paid to the Expatriate        <br /><br /><br />
Employees shall be discussed and agreed by the Parties, pursuant to Article 19.3.2 herein. The         <br /><br /><br />
Operator’s employees shall pay any individual income tax due in accordance with the provisions of      <br /><br /><br />
the individual income tax law of the People's Republic of China.                                       <br /><br /><br />

﻿ Article 21                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 Insurance                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
21.1    The Operator shall work out an insurance program for the Pilot Test Operations and                   <br /><br /><br />
submit it to JMC for review and approval within one hundred and twenty (120) days after the Date of          <br /><br /><br />
Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract. The Operator shall, on behalf of the Parties,            <br /><br /><br />
obtain the insurance contracts in accordance with such program as approved by JMC before                     <br /><br /><br />
commencement of Petroleum Operations within the Contract Area.                                               <br /><br /><br />
Similar provisions shall apply in respect of Development Operations and Production                           <br /><br /><br />
Operations.                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
21.2    All of the insurance items as approved in the insurance program shall be insured with                <br /><br /><br />
the People's Insurance Company of China or other insurance companies established within the                  <br /><br /><br />
territory of the People's Republic of China.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
21.3    The insurance programs worked out by the Operator shall include, but not be limited                  <br /><br /><br />
to, the following insurance covering:                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    damages to and expenses of all drilling installations and equipment, including                        <br /><br /><br />
damages to and expenses of the properties used on worksites and supply bases for the Petroleum               <br /><br /><br />
Operations while the equipment and properties owned by Third Party rendering services to the                 <br /><br /><br />
Operator shall be handled in accordance with Article 21.5 herein;                                            <br /><br /><br />
(b)    damages to and expenses of any of the equipment or installations for production,                      <br /><br /><br />
storage and transportation, and buildings in the course of construction and installation;                    <br /><br /><br />
(c)    damages to and expenses of the Crude Oil and/or Natural Gas production                                <br /><br /><br />
installations, facilities, equipment and pipelines;                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(d)    liability to Third Parties;                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(e)    liability for pollution and expenses for cleaning up in the course of drilling and the                <br /><br /><br />
Production Operations;                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(f)    expenses for killing blowouts;                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(g)    liability incurred by the Operator in hiring land drilling rigs, vessels and aircraft                 <br /><br /><br />
serving the Petroleum Operations;                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(h)    liability for cleaning the remains; and                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(i)    losses and expenses incurred during the transportation and storage in transit of goods                <br /><br /><br />
shipped from different parts of the world and other areas outside the Contract Area to the worksites.        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
21.4 In any insurance contracts, the deductibles shall be determined by the Parties through                  <br /><br /><br />
consultation, and losses within the deductible limits shall be borne by Parties in proportion to their       <br /><br /><br />
respective participating interests in the relevant operations.                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         n / <br /><br /><br />
﻿21.5    When signing subcontracts or lease contracts, the Operator shall endeavor to require             <br /><br /><br />
Subcontractors and lessors to insure their risks under the relevant subcontracts with the People's       <br /><br /><br />
Insurance Company of China or other insurance companies as mentioned in Article 21.2 hereof and          <br /><br /><br />
ask these Subcontractors or lessors to contact the People's Insurance Company of China or other          <br /><br /><br />
insurance companies as mentioned in Article 21.2 hereof for arrangement of the necessary insurance.      <br /><br /><br />
21.6    In the course of the Petroleum Operations, the Parties shall cover separately personnel          <br /><br /><br />
accidental death and injury insurance with respect to personnel assigned by them respectively. The       <br /><br /><br />
premiums in respect thereof shall be dealt with in the following way: the premiums for personnel         <br /><br /><br />
accidental death and injury insurance with respect to personnel whose costs are charged to the Joint     <br /><br /><br />
Account pursuant to the provisions of the Contract shall be charged to the Joint Account, and those      <br /><br /><br />
with respect to other personnel shall be borne respectively by the Parties by which they are assigned.   <br /><br /><br />
21.7    Insurance companies owned by or affiliated with any Party to the Contract, or the                <br /><br /><br />
Parties themselves, may reinsure the People's Insurance Company of China or other insurance              <br /><br /><br />
companies as mentioned in Article 21.2 herein by reaching an agreement with such company if they         <br /><br /><br />
are interested in covering any part of the insurance program hereof.                                     <br /><br /><br />
21.8    All motor vehicles used in the Petroleum Operations shall be insured with the                    <br /><br /><br />
People's Insurance Company of China or other insurance companies as mentioned in Article 21.2            <br /><br /><br />
hereof.                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
21.9    The premiums of insurance in the pilot test period and the development period shall              <br /><br /><br />
be charged to the Pilot Test Costs and the Development Costs and while those in the production           <br /><br /><br />
period shall be charged to the Operating Costs.                                                          <br /><br /><br />
21.10    Any claim under the insurance of the agreed insurance program charged to the Joint              <br /><br /><br />
Account shall be handled by the Operator and any recovery made from insurers shall be credited to        <br /><br /><br />
the Joint Account.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                              Article 22                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                     Confidentiality                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
22.1    CNPC shall, in conformity with applicable laws and regulations of the Government of                   <br /><br /><br />
the People's Republic of China on confidentiality and by taking into account international practice,          <br /><br /><br />
determine the confidentiality periods for which the Contract and all documents, information, data and         <br /><br /><br />
reports related to the Petroleum Operations within the Contract Area shall be kept confidential.              <br /><br /><br />
22.2    Without the written consent of the other Party, no Party to the Contract shall disclose,              <br /><br /><br />
during such confidentiality periods, the Contract, documents, information, data and reports referred to       <br /><br /><br />
in Article 22.1 herein or any other information regarded by JMC as confidential, to any Third Party           <br /><br /><br />
except the Third Parties specified in Articles 22.5 and 22.6 herein and to any Affiliate not directly         <br /><br /><br />
connected with the implementation of the Contract, and no Party to the Contract shall otherwise               <br /><br /><br />
transfer, donate, sell or publish them in any way within the confidentiality periods. However, if the         <br /><br /><br />
Department or Unit decides to invite any Third Party to conduct cooperative exploration and                   <br /><br /><br />
development of Petroleum in the sedimentary basin in which the Contract Area is located and/or other          <br /><br /><br />
adjacent areas, CNPC may furnish the following original data and information or interpretation                <br /><br /><br />
thereof with respect to the Contract Area to the relevant Third Parties:                                      <br /><br /><br />
(a)    original data and information held by CNPC for over two (2) years; and                                 <br /><br /><br />
(b)    interpretations to the original data and information held by CNPC for over three (3)                   <br /><br /><br />
years.                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
CNPC shall require relevant Third Parties to undertake to keep confidential the aforesaid data,               <br /><br /><br />
information, and interpretations thereof furnished to them by CNPC.                                           <br /><br /><br />
CNPC shall, in conformity with relevant provisions of laws and regulations of the People's                    <br /><br /><br />
Republic of China and requests of relevant government departments and units, provide them with all            <br /><br /><br />
documents, information, data and reports as mentioned herein.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
22.3 During the term of the Contract and after the termination of the Contract, CNPC shall                    <br /><br /><br />
not disclose to any Third Party any patent, know-how or proprietary technology transferred to CNPC            <br /><br /><br />
by the Contractor without the written consent of the Contractor except for any technology, the patent         <br /><br /><br />
of which has expired and any proprietary and confidential technology which have entered the public            <br /><br /><br />
domain.                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
22.4    After the termination of the Contract or after any assignment of rights and/or                        <br /><br /><br />
obligations of the Contract under Article 23 hereof, the Contractor and any assignee shall, within the        <br /><br /><br />
confidentiality periods, continue to be obligated to keep confidential documents, information, data and       <br /><br /><br />
reports mentioned in Article 22.2 herein except for official documents and information published with         <br /><br /><br />
the consent of the Parties.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
22.5    For the implementation of the Contract, CNPC and each company comprising the                          <br /><br /><br />
Contractor may, after review by JMC and CNPC, furnish the necessary documents, information, data              <br /><br /><br />
and reports to Third Parties and Affiliates related to the Petroleum Operations. The Third Parties and        <br /><br /><br />
Affiliates include:                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                            51                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿22.5.1    Potential investors,, banks or other credit institutions from which financing is sought         <br /><br /><br />
by any Party to the Contract for the implementation of the Contract;                                      <br /><br /><br />
22.5.2    Third Parties and Affiliates which provide services for the Petroleum Operations,               <br /><br /><br />
including Subcontractors and other service contractors; and                                               <br /><br /><br />
22.5.3    An assignee or assignees to whom the rights and/or obligations under the Contract               <br /><br /><br />
may be assigned.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
22.6    Necessary information, documents, data and reports may be furnished by the Parties                <br /><br /><br />
in accordance with the laws of their home countries to the governments and stock exchanges,               <br /><br /><br />
provided that the Parties report to JMC in advance.                                                       <br /><br /><br />
22.7    CNPC and each company comprising the Contractor when furnishing the documents,                    <br /><br /><br />
information, data and reports to Third Parties and Affiliates as mentioned in Article 22.5 herein shall   <br /><br /><br />
require them to assume the confidentiality obligations as set forth herein, or shall bear full            <br /><br /><br />
responsibility for any violation thereof.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
