﻿                                            Article 23                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                       Assignment                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
23.1 The Contractor may assign part or all of its rights and/or obligations under the                       <br /><br /><br />
Contract to any of its Affiliates with the prior consent of CNPC and in accordance with the following       <br /><br /><br />
provisions:                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(a)    The Contractor shall submit to CNPC copies of a written agreement on the                             <br /><br /><br />
corresponding part of its rights and/or obligations to be assigned;                                         <br /><br /><br />
(b)    The Contractor shall guarantee in writing to CNPC the performance of the assigned                    <br /><br /><br />
obligations; and                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(c)    No such assignment shall interfere with the performance of the Petroleum Operations                  <br /><br /><br />
or affect the organizational structure.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
23.2    The Contractor may assign part or all of its rights and/or obligations under the                    <br /><br /><br />
Contract to any Third Party, provided that such assignment shall be agreed by CNPC in advance and           <br /><br /><br />
approved by the Ministry of Foreign Trade and Economic Cooperation of the People's Republic of              <br /><br /><br />
China. However, CNPC shall have the right of first refusal in respect of such assignment provided           <br /><br /><br />
that the conditions offered by CNPC are comparable.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
23.3    CNPC may authorize its Affiliates to implement the Contract, but CNPC shall remain                  <br /><br /><br />
responsible for the performance of the Contract.                                                            <br /><br /><br />
23.4    CNPC may assign part of its rights and/or obligations hereunder to a Chinese                        <br /><br /><br />
Government controlled Third Party, provided that prior written consent of the Government of the             <br /><br /><br />
People's Republic of China shall be obtained. CNPC shall guarantee the performance of the assigned          <br /><br /><br />
obligations and that such assignment shall not interfere with the performance of Petroleum                  <br /><br /><br />
Operations.                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />

                                          53                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                            Article 24                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                           Environmental Protection and Safety                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
24.1    In the performance of the Petroleum Operations, the Operator shall be strictly subject                 <br /><br /><br />
to the laws, decrees, regulations and standards on environmental protection and safety promulgated by          <br /><br /><br />
the Chinese Government and carry out the operations according to international practice. The                   <br /><br /><br />
Operator shall make its best efforts to protect farmland, aquatic resources, forest reserves and other         <br /><br /><br />
natural resources, and prevent pollution and damage to the atmosphere, rivers, lakes, groundwater,             <br /><br /><br />
harbors, other land environments and ecological environment and secure the safety and health of the            <br /><br /><br />
operating personnel. The Operator shall use all reasonable endeavors to eliminate promptly any                 <br /><br /><br />
pollution occurring in the performance of the Petroleum Operations and minimize its consequences.              <br /><br /><br />
Economic losses caused by any pollution shall be charged to the Joint Account, unless otherwise                <br /><br /><br />
provided in Article 8.4 hereof.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
24.2    When competent authorities under die Chinese Government assign a person to inspect                     <br /><br /><br />
environmental protection and safety within the scope of the Petroleum Operations according to the              <br /><br /><br />
laws, decrees, rules and regulations, the Operator shall provide all necessary facilities and assistance       <br /><br /><br />
to enable the inspectors to carry out such inspection smoothly.                                                <br /><br /><br />
24.3    In the performance of the Petroleum Operations in any fixed fishing net casting area                   <br /><br /><br />
and/or aquatic breeding area, the Operator shall make prior contact with the relevant authorities of the       <br /><br /><br />
Chinese Government.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
24.4    Before the commencement of Pilot Test Operations, the Operator shall provide CNPC                      <br /><br /><br />
with documentation on the possible impact by the Pilot Test Operations on the environment and                  <br /><br /><br />
measures to be adopted to prevent pollution.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
24.5    The Operator shall, after the completion of various Petroleum Operations, level or                     <br /><br /><br />
restore or reclaim the land of the operating sites in accordance with the relevant local rules and             <br /><br /><br />
regulations, provided that CNPC shall be responsible for any environmental damage caused and any               <br /><br /><br />
restoration required, as a result of any work performed in the Contract Area prior to the effective date       <br /><br /><br />
of this Contract.                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                            Article 25                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                      Force Majeure                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
25.1    No Party to the Contract shall be considered in default of the performance of any of                   <br /><br /><br />
its obligations hereunder, if any failure to perform or any delay in performing its obligations is in          <br /><br /><br />
conformity with all the events described as follows:                                                           <br /><br /><br />
The performance of any obligations hereunder is prevented, hindered or delayed because of                      <br /><br /><br />
any event or combination of events which could not be foreseen and/or which is beyond the control of           <br /><br /><br />
such Party;                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
Any such event or combination of events is the direct cause of preventing, hindering or                        <br /><br /><br />
delaying of such Party's performance of its obligations hereunder; and                                         <br /><br /><br />
When any such event or combination of events has occurred, such P<irty has taken all                           <br /><br /><br />
reasonable actions to overcome any cause that prevents, hinders or delays performance of its                   <br /><br /><br />
obligations and shall in so far as is practicable continue to perform its obligations hereunder.               <br /><br /><br />
25.2    Notice of any event of force majeure and the conclusion thereof shall forthwith be                     <br /><br /><br />
given to the other Party by the Party claiming force majeure.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
25.3    In the event of force majeure, the Parties shall immediately consult in order to find an               <br /><br /><br />
equitable solution thereto and shall use all reasonable endeavors to minimize the consequences of              <br /><br /><br />
such force majeure.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
25.4    If the Petroleum Operations in the Contract Area are partially or entirely suspended as                <br /><br /><br />
a result of the force majeure referred to in Article 25.1 herein, the period of the Petroleum Operations       <br /><br /><br />
may be extended by a period equal to the corresponding period of such suspension. Within fifteen               <br /><br /><br />
(15) days following the end of each Calendar Year, the Operator shall report to JMC in writing on the          <br /><br /><br />
suspension of the Petroleum Operations caused by force majeure, if any, during the preceding                   <br /><br /><br />
Calendar Year.                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
25.5    The provisions of this Article 25 shall not apply in the case of default in the making                 <br /><br /><br />
of any payments of money.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

                                         55                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                            Article 26                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                Consultation and Arbitration                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
26.1    The Parties shall make their best efforts to settle amicably through consultation any                      <br /><br /><br />
dispute arising in connection with the performance or interpretation of any provision hereof.                      <br /><br /><br />
26.2    Any dispute mentioned in Article 26.1 herein that has not been settled through such                        <br /><br /><br />
consultation within ninety (90) days after the dispute arises may be referred to arbitration at the                <br /><br /><br />
request of and by either Party to the Contract. The arbitration shall be conducted in accordance with              <br /><br /><br />
the following provisions:                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
26.2.1    If agreed upon by the Parties, such dispute shall be referred to arbitration conducted                   <br /><br /><br />
by the China International Economic and Trade Arbitration Commission in accordance with the                        <br /><br /><br />
arbitration proceeding rules thereof.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
26.2.2    If the Parties fail to reach an agreement on the arbitration arrangement mentioned in                    <br /><br /><br />
Article 26.2.1 herein, the Parties shall establish an ad hoc arbitration tribunal to conduct arbitration in        <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the following provisions:                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
26.2.2.1    The ad hoc arbitration tribunal shall consist of three (3) arbitrators The Parties shall               <br /><br /><br />
each appoint an arbitrator and the two arbitrators so appointed shall designate a third arbitrator. If one         <br /><br /><br />
of the Parties does not appoint its arbitrator within sixty (60) days after the first appointment, or if the       <br /><br /><br />
two arbitrators once appointed fail to appoint the third within sixty (60) days after the appointment of           <br /><br /><br />
the second arbitrator, the relevant appointment shall be made by the Arbitration Institute of the                  <br /><br /><br />
Stockholm Chamber of Commerce, Sweden.                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
26.2.2.2    The third arbitrator shall be a citizen of a country which has formal diplomatic                       <br /><br /><br />
relations with both the People’s Republic of China and the home country of any of companies                        <br /><br /><br />
comprising the Contractor, and shall not have any economic interests or relationship with the Parties.             <br /><br /><br />
26.2.2.3    The place of arbitration shall be determined by the Parties through consultations or,                  <br /><br /><br />
failing the agreement of the Parties within sixty (60) days after the appointment of the third arbitrator,         <br /><br /><br />
by the majority of arbitrators of the ad hoc arbitration tribunal.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
26.2.2.4    The ad hoc arbitration tribunal shall conduct the arbitration in accordance with the                   <br /><br /><br />
arbitration rules of the United Nations Commission on International Trade Law (;‘UNCITRAL”) of                     <br /><br /><br />
1976. However, if the above-mentioned arbitration rules are in conflict with the provisions of this                <br /><br /><br />
Article 26, including the provisions concerning appointment of arbitrators, the provisions of this                 <br /><br /><br />
Article 26 shall prevail.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
26.3    Both the Chinese and English languages shall be official languages used in the                             <br /><br /><br />
arbitral proceedings. All hearing materials, statements of claim or defense, awards and the reasons                <br /><br /><br />
supporting them shall be written in both Chinese and English.                                                      <br /><br /><br />
26.4    Any award of the arbitration tribunal shall be final and binding upon the Parties.                         <br /><br /><br />
26.5    The right to arbitrate disputes under the Contract shall survive the termination of the                    <br /><br /><br />
Contract.                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                         56                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿                            Article 27                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 Effectiveness and Termination of the Contract                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
27.1    After it is signed, the Contract shall be approved by the Ministry of Foreign Trade                   <br /><br /><br />
and Economic Cooperation of the People s Republic of China. The date of such approval shall be the            <br /><br /><br />
effective date of the Contract. However, the Contractor's obligations shall begin on the Date of              <br /><br /><br />
Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract, as defined in Article 1.40, herein above.                 <br /><br /><br />
CNPC shall notify the Contractor of the said approval in writing as soon as possible.                         <br /><br /><br />
27.2    All annexes to the Contract shall be regarded as integral parts of the Contract. If there             <br /><br /><br />
is any inconsistency between the provisions of the annexes and the main body of the Contract, the             <br /><br /><br />
main body of the Contract shall prevail. All references to the Contract hereof refer to the main body         <br /><br /><br />
of the Contract.                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
27.3    If in the course of implementation of the Contract, the Parties decide through                        <br /><br /><br />
consultation to make amendment or supplement to any part of the Contract, a written agreement                 <br /><br /><br />
signed by the authorized representatives of the Parties shall be required. Such written agreement shall       <br /><br /><br />
be subject to the approval of the Ministry of Foreign Trade and Economic Cooperation of the People's          <br /><br /><br />
Republic of China should there be any significant modifications hereof. Such agreement shall be               <br /><br /><br />
regarded as an integral part of the Contract.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
27.4    The Contract shall terminate under any of the following circumstances;                                <br /><br /><br />
27.4.1    The Contractor opts to terminate the Contract in accordance with Article 6.3 (2)                    <br /><br /><br />
herein; or                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
27.4.2    on the termination date of the production period of the Oil Field; or                               <br /><br /><br />
27.4.3    at the end of the last day of the thirtieth (30th) Contract Year from the Date of                   <br /><br /><br />
Commencement of the Implementation of the Contract, unless the production period is extended by               <br /><br /><br />
the approval of the Department or Unit under Article 4.3 hereof or unless otherwise stipulated in             <br /><br /><br />
Articles 4.6.1 or 25.4 hereof.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
27.5    If either Party to the Contract commits a material breach of the Contract, the other                  <br /><br /><br />
Party to the Contract shall have the right to demand that such breach be remedied within a reasonably         <br /><br /><br />
specified period of time. If such breach is not remedied within such period of time, the complaining          <br /><br /><br />
Party shall have the right to terminate the Contract by giving ninety (90) days written notice to the         <br /><br /><br />
defaulting Party. However, such material breach of the Contract and unremedied material breach                <br /><br /><br />
shall have been judged by a final award of arbitration in accordance with Article 26 hereof.                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />

﻿                       Article 28                                                                             <br /><br /><br />

 The Applicable Law                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
28.1    The validity, interpretation and implementation of the Contract shall be governed by                  <br /><br /><br />
the laws of the People's Republic of China. Failing the relevant provisions of the laws of the People's       <br /><br /><br />
Republic of China for the interpretation or implementation of the Contract, the principles of the             <br /><br /><br />
applicable laws widely used in Petroleum resource countries acceptable to the Parties shall be                <br /><br /><br />
applicable.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
28.2    If a material change occurs to the Contractor's economic benefits after the effective                 <br /><br /><br />
date of the Contract due to the promulgation of new laws, decrees, rules and regulations or any               <br /><br /><br />
amendment to the applicable laws, decrees, rules and regulations made by the People's Republic of             <br /><br /><br />
China, the Parties shall consult promptly and make necessary revisions and adjustments to the                 <br /><br /><br />
relevant provisions of the Contract in order to maintain the Contractor's reasonable economic benefits        <br /><br /><br />
hereunder.                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />

29.1    The text of the Contract, annexes and supplementary documents attached hereto shall                 <br /><br /><br />
be written in both Chinese and English, and both versions shall have equal force and effect.                <br /><br /><br />
29.2    The Parties agree that both Chinese and English shall be used as working languages.                 <br /><br /><br />
After the effective date of the Contract, technical documents and information concerning the                <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations hereunder shall, in general, be written in English except for technical                <br /><br /><br />
documents and information available previously and received from Third Parties.                             <br /><br /><br />
Unless otherwise agreed by CNPC, documents and information in respect of administration                     <br /><br /><br />
shall be written in both Chinese and English. Forms for production and other reports and records            <br /><br /><br />
shall be printed with headings in both Chinese and English and may be filled out in either Chinese or       <br /><br /><br />
English.                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                              Annex II                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                  Accounting Procedure                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
        Article 1 General Provisions                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
       1.1    This Accounting Procedure is an integral part of the Contract.                                                <br /><br /><br />
• s                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
       The definitions set forth in Article 1 of the Contract are equally applicable to this Accounting                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
       Procedure. The definitions and provisions in this Accounting Procedure have the same force and                       <br /><br /><br />
       effect as those in the Contract. If the provisions in this Accounting Procedure are in conflict with                 <br /><br /><br />
       those in the Contract, the provisions in the Contract shall prevail.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                         ii <br /><br /><br />
m      1.2    Purpose: The purpose of this Accounting Procedure is to establish equitable control                        i  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                         i  <br /><br /><br />
n ■    methods for determining charges and credits applicable to the Petroleum Operations according to the                  <br /><br /><br />
•4 j   relevant provisions of the Contract, including the guidelines for accounting settlements in respect of               <br /><br /><br />
       managing funds and materials, financing and Accounting Records, and for compiling accounting                         <br /><br /><br />
       statements.                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
       1.3 Accounting methods: The double-entry method of accounting shall be used in this                                  <br /><br /><br />
       Accounting Procedure.                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
       1.4    Working language: Chinese or both Chinese and English shall be used as the working                            <br /><br /><br />
       languages for the Accounting Records and analyses of financial conditions in respect of the Joint                    <br /><br /><br />
       Account, at the Operator's option.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
       1.5    Currency for accounting: U.S. Dollars shall be the unit of currency for accounting in                         <br /><br /><br />
       the Joint Account and shall be the currency for the investments and reimbursements under, the                        <br /><br /><br />
       Contract. In case currencies other than U.S. Dollars are used to carry out business activities, the                  <br /><br /><br />
       relevant bank accounts and other current asset and current liability accounts shall be kept both in U.S.             <br /><br /><br />
       Dollars and in the currencies used.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
       1.6 Currency translation: For the purpose of accounting, currency translation entered                                <br /><br /><br />
       into the Joint Account shall be made in accordance with following guidelines:                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
       The rate of exchange to be used for the conversion into U.S. Dollars of cash calls received in                       <br /><br /><br />
       Renminbi shall be the arithmetic average of buying and selling rates of exchange applicable to any                   <br /><br /><br />
       individual or commercial entity quoted by Bank of China at 11:00 a.m. on the date of receipt of such                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                          66                                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿cash in the Operator's bank account(s). If the relevant date is a non-business day of the Bank of          <br /><br /><br />
China, the rate quoted on the previous business day by the Bank of China shall apply.                      <br /><br /><br />
All other transactions recorded in the Joint Account which are made in Renminbi shall be                   <br /><br /><br />
translated into and recorded in U.S. Dollars at the rate of exchange as quoted above on the last           <br /><br /><br />
business day of the previous month, while those transactions which are made in currencies other than       <br /><br /><br />
Renminbi and U.S. Dollars shall be recorded in U.S. Dollars at the actual cost in U.S. Dollars of          <br /><br /><br />
effecting the transaction.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Neither CNPC nor the companies comprising the Contractor shall experience an exchange                      <br /><br /><br />
gain or loss, at the expense or benefit of the other Party.                                                <br /><br /><br />
The Operator shall make its best efforts to minimize any exchange loss.                                    <br /><br /><br />
All gains or losses from currency conversion or translation shall be recorded in the Joint                 <br /><br /><br />
Account.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
1.7    Foreign exchange business: Foreign exchange business related to the Petroleum                       <br /><br /><br />
Operations shall be made in accordance with “Regulations for Exchange Control of the People's              <br /><br /><br />
Republic of China” and “Rules for the Implementation of Exchange Control Regulation Relating to            <br /><br /><br />
Enterprises with Overseas Chinese Capital, Enterprises with Foreign Capital, and Chinese and               <br /><br /><br />
Foreign Joint Ventures.”                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
1.8    Accounting Records and statements:                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
1.8.1    All Accounting Records related to the Petroleum Operations shall be established and               <br /><br /><br />
maintained by the Operator within the territory of the People's Republic of China.                         <br /><br /><br />
1.8.2    All vouchers, accounts, books and statements shall be prepared in accordance with                 <br /><br /><br />
the Petroleum Operations Accounting System established by CNPC and the Contractor through                  <br /><br /><br />
consultation pursuant to the “Accounting Regulations of the People's Republic of China for                 <br /><br /><br />
Enterprises with Foreign Investment”.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.8.3    Annual accounting statements and important accounting books, including asset                      <br /><br /><br />
records; cash or bank journals, general and subsidiary ledgers, balance sheets, and annual gross oil       <br /><br /><br />
production allocation statements shall be maintained for the term of the Contract as per Article 4.7 of    <br /><br /><br />
the Contract, or for any further period if required by the laws and regulations of the People's Republic   <br /><br /><br />
of China. Other accounting vouchers and books shall be kept for fifteen (15) years. Quarterly and          <br /><br /><br />
monthly statements shall be maintained for five (5) years.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 67                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿   Upon the expiration of the custody period, a list shall be made of the accounting files to be               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
   disposed of. Disposal of the accounting files shall only be made after the approval of CNPC. The list       <br /><br /><br />
   of the accounting files disposed of shall be maintained with the annual accounting statements.              <br /><br /><br />

﻿                             Article 2 Definitions                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
The terms used in this Accounting Procedure shall have the definitions ascribed to them as                   <br /><br /><br />
follows:                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
2.1    “Accounting Records” means all accounting books, source documents, original                           <br /><br /><br />
vouchers, approved documents, analytical data, work papers and accounting statements maintained              <br /><br /><br />
for the Petroleum Operations.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
2.2    “Accounting System” means the Petroleum Operations Accounting System prepared                         <br /><br /><br />
by CNPC and the Contractor through consultation pursuant to the “Accounting Regulations of the               <br /><br /><br />
People's Republic of China for Enterprises with Foreign Investment”, specifying the accounting titles        <br /><br /><br />
to be used by the Operator and instructions for implementation, forms and contents of various                <br /><br /><br />
accounting statements and their preparation methods, including a material classification section, a          <br /><br /><br />
definition of Controllable Material, standards for itemizing assets and the provisions for fixed asset       <br /><br /><br />
accounting.                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
2.3    “Material” means materials, tools, facilities, equipment and consumables procured,                    <br /><br /><br />
leased or otherwise acquired and held for the Petroleum Operations.                                          <br /><br /><br />
2.4    “Joint Account” means accounts established by the Operator for the implementation                     <br /><br /><br />
of the Contract to record all debts and credits related to the Petroleum Operations.                         <br /><br /><br />
2.5    “Controllable Material” means the Material referred to in the Accounting System                       <br /><br /><br />
described in Article 2.2 of this Accounting Procedure.                                                       <br /><br /><br />
2.6    “LIBOR” means the seven-day term London Inter-Bank Offered Rate for U.S.                              <br /><br /><br />
Dollars for similar amounts to the sums in question, quoted by Midland Bank in London at 11:00 a.m.          <br /><br /><br />
on the first business day of the relevant period                                                             <br /><br /><br />
2.7    “Investing Party” means any party that is contributing the funds for the Petroleum                    <br /><br /><br />
Operations in accordance with its participating interest determined pursuant to the relevant provisions      <br /><br /><br />
of the Contract.                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                             69                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
﻿                               Article 3 Cash Calls                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
3.1 Except as otherwise provided in the Contract, the Contractor shall solely provide all                    <br /><br /><br />
the Pilot Test Costs and all the Development Costs according to the provision of Articles 12.1.1 and         <br /><br /><br />
12.1.2 of the Contract. In accordance with each approved annual budget, the Operator shall issue             <br /><br /><br />
monthly cash call notices to each company comprising the Contractor to provide the Operator with             <br /><br /><br />
funds to cover the planned expenditures of the next month. Whether or not the cash call notices for          <br /><br /><br />
the Pilot Test Costs are to be issued shall be at the option of the Operator.                                <br /><br /><br />
3.2 Development Operations cash call and default                                                             <br /><br /><br />
3.2.1    According to the needs of the Petroleum Operations, the Operator shall regularly                    <br /><br /><br />
issue monthly cash call notices within the amount of approved annual budget to request each company          <br /><br /><br />
comprising the Contractor to respectively make advances as specified by the Operator. The Operator           <br /><br /><br />
shall, before twenty (20) days prior to the commencement of each month, issue cash call notices for          <br /><br /><br />
the Development Costs and each company comprising the Contractor shall provide its percentage                <br /><br /><br />
share of funds according to the requirement and within the time limit specified in the cash call notice.     <br /><br /><br />
However the payment due date specified in the cash call notices shall not be earlier than the first          <br /><br /><br />
working day of the month for which cash is called. Each company comprising the Contractor shall              <br /><br /><br />
transfer its percentage share of funds to the Operator's bank accounts) established by the Operator          <br /><br /><br />
particularly for the Petroleum Operations. Such bank account(s) will in all cases be interest bearing        <br /><br /><br />
accounts).                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
Any excessive advances made by each Company comprising the Contractor for any month                          <br /><br /><br />
shall be adjusted in the next cash call.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
In case that the Operator, owing to the needs of the Development Operations, has to incur                    <br /><br /><br />
expenditures which are unforeseen in the cash call for any month, written notices shall be issued to all     <br /><br /><br />
the companies comprising the Contractor who shall finance their own shares or additional amount              <br /><br /><br />
within ten (10) days following die receipt of the written notice.                                            <br /><br /><br />
3.2.2    Interest shall be paid by the companies comprising the Contractor failing to pay its                <br /><br /><br />
share of funds on the due date specified in the cash call at LIBOR on the delinquent date plus five          <br /><br /><br />
percent (5%) on the delinquency of less than one (1) month and thereafter at the average LIBOR rate          <br /><br /><br />
ruling throughout each subsequent month plus five percent (5%), such interest being compounded on            <br /><br /><br />
a monthly basis throughout the period of the delinquency. The non-defaulting party or parties shall          <br /><br /><br />
make up the delinquent portion on behalf of the defaulting party or parties. When the defaulting party       <br /><br /><br />
or parties pay cash to meet both the delinquent portion and accrued interest thereon, the Operator shall     <br /><br /><br />
reimburse the non-defaulting party or parties who made up the delinquent portion.                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                70                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿All amounts advanced by the non-defaulting party or parties plus accrued interest not                       <br /><br /><br />
reimbursed by the defaulting party shall constitute a debt due from the defaulting party or parties to      <br /><br /><br />
the non-defaulting party or parties who shall be entitled to all remedies at law and equity. Any non¬       <br /><br /><br />
defaulting party shall, on behalf of the non-defaulting party or parties be entitled to take and sell the   <br /><br /><br />
defaulting party’s or parties’ share of the Annual Gross Production of Crude Oil and apply the              <br /><br /><br />
proceeds of the sale of such Crude Oil against all sums due and payable by the defaulting party or          <br /><br /><br />
parties including accrued interest. Any excess funds remaining from such proceeds after deduction of        <br /><br /><br />
all amounts due, including interest and the costs, charges and expenses incurred by any non-defaulting      <br /><br /><br />
party, in connection with such sale, shall be paid over to the defaulting party. Any deficiency             <br /><br /><br />
remaining due after deducting the proceeds of any such sale shall remain an obligation of the               <br /><br /><br />
defaulting party or parties and may be collected as any other debt.                                         <br /><br /><br />
3.3 Each monthly cash call notice shall clearly indicate the following information:                         <br /><br /><br />
3.3.1    Annual Development Costs to be shared by each company comprising the Contractor                    <br /><br /><br />
as shown in the approved annual budget.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
3.3.2    Amount of funds advanced by each company comprising of the Contractor at the end                   <br /><br /><br />
of the month prior to the month in which the cash call notice is prepared and the actual expenditures       <br /><br /><br />
and the actual balance (i.e. funds unused) recorded in the Joint Account, accompanied by the bank           <br /><br /><br />
statements related to the Joint Account for the previous month.                                             <br /><br /><br />
3.3.3. Amount of funds to be called from each company comprising the Contractor in the                      <br /><br /><br />
month for which the funds will be used and the estimated amounts of funds to be called in the               <br /><br /><br />
following two (2) months.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
3.3.4    The date when funds are to be provided, the amount of funds, currency, account                     <br /><br /><br />
number, name of the account, the recipient bank and its address.                                            <br /><br /><br />
3.4    On the Date of Commencement of Commercial Production of the Oil Field,.any                           <br /><br /><br />
development investment for the Oil Field advanced by the company comprising the Contractor which            <br /><br /><br />
has not been expended or will not be expended shall be returned to each of the companies in                 <br /><br /><br />
proportion to its share.                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
3.5    The cash for the Production Operations undertaken by the Parties jointly and                         <br /><br /><br />
approved by JMC shall be provided by all the Investing Parties to the Contract according to Article         <br /><br /><br />
12.1.3 of the Contract, but the Contractor shall, in accordance with Article 12.1.3 of the Contract, pay    <br /><br /><br />
for CNPC the Operating Costs which shall be paid by CNPC. Based on the needs of the Production              <br /><br /><br />
Operations, the Operator may make timely adjustment of the amount of cash to be provided by all the         <br /><br /><br />
Investing Parties to the Contract. The Operator shall issue quarterly cash call notices to call for cash    <br /><br /><br />
for the Production Operations. In proportion to its share, each Investing Party shall respectively          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 71                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
﻿provide advances on a monthly basis in accordance with the requirement and within the time limit             <br /><br /><br />
specified in the cash call notice of the current month.                                                      <br /><br /><br />
In case that the Operator, owing to the needs of the Production Operations, has to incur                     <br /><br /><br />
expenditures which are unforeseen in the cash call for any month, written notices with explanations          <br /><br /><br />
shall be issued to all the Investing Parties who shall finance their own shares for additional amount        <br /><br /><br />
within ten (10) days following the receipt of such written notice.                                           <br /><br /><br />
3.6    According to the requirement of the Petroleum Operations, the Operator shall indicate                 <br /><br /><br />
in any cash call notice the U.S. Dollar equivalent of the total cash called. The Operator shall also         <br /><br /><br />
specify the amounts of Renminbi and U.S. Dollars required as estimated to make payment.                      <br /><br /><br />
3.7    Provisions for recording the sources of funds:                                                        <br /><br /><br />
3.7.1    Funds for Pilot Test Costs, Development Costs and Operating Costs, when received,                   <br /><br /><br />
pursuant to each cash call shall be credited against the relevant accounts of the Investing Parties in the   <br /><br /><br />
Joint Account.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
3.7.2    In case either Party to the Contract decides to develop excess Associated Natural Gas               <br /><br /><br />
for its sole account pursuant to Article 18.1.2.3 of the Contract, or undertakes any other operation for     <br /><br /><br />
its sole account, the funds required shall be financed and accounted for separately.                         <br /><br /><br />
3.7.3    The Contractor shall, within twenty (20) days after the date of submission to CNPC                  <br /><br /><br />
of a written notice expressing its decision to participate in the utilization of the excess Associated       <br /><br /><br />
Natural Gas of the Oil Field undertaken solely by CNPC, pay CNPC in cash the amounts stipulated in           <br /><br /><br />
Article 18.1.2.3 of the Contract.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
3.7.4    In accordance with Article 6.5 of the Contract, if the Contractor opts to terminate the             <br /><br /><br />
Contract as provided in Article 6.3 (2) of the Contract, the Contractor shall, within thirty (30) days       <br /><br /><br />
from the date of the expiration of the pilot test period, pay CNPC in U.S. Dollars the unfulfilled           <br /><br /><br />
balance of the minimum pilot test work commitment stipulated in the pilot test period, converted, into       <br /><br /><br />
cash. The detailed method by which the unfulfilled balance of the minimum pilot test work                    <br /><br /><br />
commitment is converted into U.S. Dollars is that the actual average unit cost of the last portion of the    <br /><br /><br />
work under the Contract or of the last well drilled, excluding the abnormal drilling costs such as those     <br /><br /><br />
of fishing, severe loss of mud circulation, etc. is multiplied by the unfulfilled amount of the minimum      <br /><br /><br />
pilot test work commitment. The formula for such calculation is as follows:                                  <br /><br /><br />
I = Ac x Pu                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
in which:                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 72                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
﻿I = converted cash amount of the unfulfilled balance of the minimum pilot test work                         <br /><br /><br />
commitment;                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Ac = actual average unit cost of the last portion of the work or of the last well drilled (If there is      <br /><br /><br />
no average unit cost, the estimated unit costs or expenses in the pilot test program shall be applied for   <br /><br /><br />
calculating); and                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
Pu = the unfulfilled amount of the minimum pilot test work commitment (The unfulfilled                      <br /><br /><br />
amount of the work is the difference between the work specified in Article 6.2.1 of the Contract and        <br /><br /><br />
actual work.)                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

 73                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
﻿                  Article 4 Accounting and Management of Material                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
4.1    Procurement of Material:                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
The procurement of Material shall be implemented in accordance with the procedure specified                    <br /><br /><br />
in Articles 15.1 and 7.6 of the Contract. In order to prevent overstocking of Material, the Operator           <br /><br /><br />
shall use all reasonable best efforts to ensure that the procurement of Material shall be made in              <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the Material procurement plans and that the quality of material conforms to                    <br /><br /><br />
specifications and prices are fair and reasonable. The Operator does not warrant the Materials                 <br /><br /><br />
furnished beyond, or back of, the supplier's or manufacturer's guarantee.                                      <br /><br /><br />
4.2    Costs of procuring Material                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
The costs of Material purchased shall be the invoice prices less discounts plus related                        <br /><br /><br />
transportation and other expenses, including expenses for freight to the destination, insurance                <br /><br /><br />
premiums commensurate with the material covered, fees of forwarding agents, duties, fees, handling             <br /><br /><br />
expenses from shipside to and within any water or land terminal warehouse or yard, and any other               <br /><br /><br />
reasonable expenses actually paid and expenses of inland transportation.                                       <br /><br /><br />
4.3    The provisions and procedures of Article 15.1 and Article 7.6 of the Contract and the                   <br /><br /><br />
following provisions shall be applied for pricing Material furnished from the stocks of the Parties            <br /><br /><br />
and/or their Affiliates for use in the Petroleum Operations:                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(1)    New Material:                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
New Material shall be priced on the basis of current market value plus expenses in moving                      <br /><br /><br />
such Material directly to the job-site where Material is used.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(2)    Used Material:                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Material which is in sound and serviceable condition and is suitable for reuse without                  <br /><br /><br />
reconditioning shall be priced by the Parties, and the ceiling price shall not exceed seventy-five             <br /><br /><br />
percent (75%) of the current market value of new Material.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Material which, after being reconditioned, will be further serviceable for its original                 <br /><br /><br />
function shall be priced by the Parties, and the ceiling price shall not exceed fifty percent (50%) of the     <br /><br /><br />
current value of new Material.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Used Material which cannot be classified as (a) or (b) above shall be priced by the                     <br /><br /><br />
Parties through discussions at a value commensurate with its use.                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                               74                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
﻿(d) If the Operator wishes to use a method other than the above for pricing used Material,              <br /><br /><br />
such other method shall be agreed upon in advance by the Parties through consultations.                 <br /><br /><br />
4.4    Price determination and leasing expense calculation method for properties purchased              <br /><br /><br />
or leased from other contract areas:                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
The Operator may lease equipment and facilities and purchase Material and fuel from other               <br /><br /><br />
contract areas within the People's Republic of China. The Operator shall charge the leasing expenses    <br /><br /><br />
or purchase price as agreed upon by the Operator and its suppliers. Such leasing expenses or purchase   <br /><br /><br />
prices shall not exceed those currently prevailing in similar contract areas.                           <br /><br /><br />
4.5    For certain Material which is in short supply in the world markets and difficult to              <br /><br /><br />
procure at published market prices and the lack of which will hinder normal operations, the Operator    <br /><br /><br />
may, after the approval of JMC, purchase such Material urgently needed by the Petroleum Operations      <br /><br /><br />
and charge actual purchase costs to the Joint Account.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
4.6    Disposal of Equipment and Material:                                                              <br /><br /><br />
The Operator shall not dispose of or sell Material with book value exceeding Ten Thousand               <br /><br /><br />
U.S. Dollars (U.S.$ 10,000) without the prior consent of the Parties. The Operator shall use all        <br /><br /><br />
reasonable endeavors to minimize losses in the disposal of or sales of such Material.                   <br /><br /><br />
Sales of properties to Third Parties or Affiliates shall be recorded in accordance with actual          <br /><br /><br />
sales income. No guaranty or warranty for Material sold or disposed of under this Article shall be      <br /><br /><br />
given by the Operator to any purchaser.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
4.7    Accounting for Material:                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
The costs of Material which is procured by the Operator and is directly used at the job-site            <br /><br /><br />
shall be charged to the respective accounts of Pilot Test Costs, Development Costs or Operating Costs   <br /><br /><br />
at actual purchase prices (as defined in Article 4.2 herein) and on the basis of the use of Material.   <br /><br /><br />
Should such Material subsequently be used for other purposes, the relevant charges shall be             <br /><br /><br />
transferred from the original cost accounts to the appropriate cost accounts.                           <br /><br /><br />
Material for general use which is first stored in warehouses shall be subject to inventory              <br /><br /><br />
control procedures. The quantities, unit prices and total value shall be recorded for Material in       <br /><br /><br />
inventory using perpetual inventory methods. Material in stock shall be priced at purchase costs and    <br /><br /><br />
the Operator, upon the commencement of or during the Contract period, has the freedom to choose         <br /><br /><br />
one of the following pricing methods such as FIFO, weighted average method and moving average           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 75                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
﻿method, etc. for Material to be transferred out of the stock. Accounts for inventory Material shall be        <br /><br /><br />
regarded as Pilot Test Costs, Development Costs or Operating Costs.                                           <br /><br /><br />
At the request of any Party of the Contract, the Operator shall furnish to such Party a detailed              <br /><br /><br />
statement of Controllable Material.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
The Operator shall conduct a physical inventory of Material in warehouses prior to the annual                 <br /><br /><br />
final accounts or whenever depending upon the actual situation. The Operator shall give a written             <br /><br /><br />
notice to JMC sixty (60) days before the date of proposed physical inventory in order to allow time           <br /><br /><br />
for participation by each Party of the Contract and failure to participate by any Party of the Contract       <br /><br /><br />
in the physical inventory shall be regarded as approval of the physical inventory conducted by the            <br /><br /><br />
Operator.                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
If any gain or loss is found as a result of the physical inventory, the Operator shall compile a              <br /><br /><br />
detailed statement of the gain or loss and attach to it an explanation for the gain or loss, which shall be   <br /><br /><br />
submitted to JMC for examination and approval.                                                                <br /><br /><br />
4.8 In accordance with Article 17.1 of the Contract, the Operator shall exercise strict                       <br /><br /><br />
control over the fixed assets of the Petroleum Operations and set up accounts and record cards, and           <br /><br /><br />
shall conduct a physical inventory of the fixed assets at the year-end or whenever depending upon the         <br /><br /><br />
actual situation to make sure that the book records, card records and physical fixed assets are in            <br /><br /><br />
conformity. In case that any damage or loss arises to the fixed assets, the Operator shall determine the      <br /><br /><br />
reasons and submit them to JMC for examination and approval.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
