5.2.9    Taxes:                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
All taxes paid according to the tax laws of the People's Republic of China, except for the                <br /><br /><br />
income taxes, Value Added Tax and Royalty to be paid by the companies comprising the Contractor           <br /><br /><br />
or CNPC.                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
5.2.10    Energy expenses:                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
All costs in respect of fuel, electricity, heat, water or other energy used and consumed for the          <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
5.2.11    Field office facility charges:                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
The costs and expenses of establishing, maintaining and operating any offices, camps or                   <br /><br /><br />
housing facilities necessary for the performance of job-site operations, including a share of the costs   <br /><br /><br />
of any office used by staff directing such operations (calculated by apportioning office costs and        <br /><br /><br />
expenses on the basis of space occupied by such staff).                                                   <br /><br /><br />
5.2.12    Communication charges:                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
The costs of acquiring, leasing, installing, operating, repairing and maintaining                         <br /><br /><br />
communication systems, including radio and microwave facilities between the Contract Area and the         <br /><br /><br />
base facilities.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
5.2.13    Ecological and environmental protection charges:                                                <br /><br /><br />
The charges for any measures undertaken for the Petroleum Operations within the Contract                  <br /><br /><br />
Area as required by relevant statutory regulations formulated by the authorities concerned or pursuant    <br /><br /><br />
to the programs agreed by the Parties.                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
5.2.14    Service charges:                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
5.2.14.1 Technical service:                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
The charges paid for services, such as rock specimen analysis, oil quality tests, geological              <br /><br /><br />
evaluation, data processing, design and engineering, well site geology, drilling supervision, special     <br /><br /><br />
research programs and other technical services.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 79                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
﻿ 5.2 Cost items:                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
The following items shall be chargeable to the Joint Account at Operator's net cost.                        <br /><br /><br />
5.2.1    Subcontractor charges:                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
The charges paid to Subcontractors in accordance with contracts signed between the Operator                 <br /><br /><br />
and Subcontractors.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
5.2.2    Personnel expenses:                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
The contents and control of personnel expenses including but not limited to reimbursable                    <br /><br /><br />
individual income taxes, provided that Contractor will supply supporting information for such taxes,        <br /><br /><br />
shall be stipulated in Article 19.3 of the Contract.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
5.2.3    Travel and living expenses:                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
Travel and living expenses paid according to Article 19 of the Contract to the personnel                    <br /><br /><br />
involved in the Petroleum Operations.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
5.2.4    Material expenses:                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Expenses paid in accordance with Article 4 of this Accounting Procedure to purchase                         <br /><br /><br />
Material for use in the Petroleum Operations.                                                               <br /><br /><br />
5.2.5    Relocation and transportation expenses:                                                            <br /><br /><br />
Relocation and transportation expenses for the personnel involved in the Petroleum                          <br /><br /><br />
Operations to be relocated into or out of the People's Republic of China and transferred from job-sites     <br /><br /><br />
to job-sites within the People's Republic of China.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
5.2.6    Maintenance, repair and leasing expenses:                                                          <br /><br /><br />
Expenses for maintenance, repair or replacement of the properties used in the Petroleum                     <br /><br /><br />
Operations and the leasing expenses paid for leased properties and equipment.                               <br /><br /><br />
5.2.7    Insurance premiums:                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
Necessary net payment made for the insurance of the Petroleum Operations and related costs                  <br /><br /><br />
and expenses, including deductibles paid in the event of loss pursuant to Article 21.4 of the Contract.     <br /><br /><br />
5.2.8    Legal expenses:    1                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                  78                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿ 5.2.14.2 General service charges:                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
Professional consultant charges incurred for the common interests of both Parties and charges             <br /><br /><br />
for other services to obtain original data needed for Petroleum Operations from outside sources,          <br /><br /><br />
except legal service.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
5.2.14.3 CNPC’s assistance charges:                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(a)    The charges for the assistance provided by CNPC for the Contractor to carry out the                <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations in accordance with Article 9 of the Contract.                                        <br /><br /><br />
(b)    For all assistance to be provided by the head office organization of CNPC to the                   <br /><br /><br />
Contractor in the course of the Development Operations, CNPC shall charge an administrative fee of        <br /><br /><br />
One Hundred and Seventy-five Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$175,000) for each Calendar Year. The               <br /><br /><br />
aforesaid administrative fee shall be paid respectively on June 1st and December 1st each Calendar        <br /><br /><br />
Year, with Eighty-seven Thousand and Five Hundred U.S. Dollars (US$87,500) for each time.                 <br /><br /><br />
(c)    For all assistance to be provided by the head office organization of CNPC to the                   <br /><br /><br />
Contractor in the course of the Production Operations before CNPC takes over the said Production          <br /><br /><br />
Operations, CNPC shall charge an administrative fee of: Two Hundred and Fifty Thousand U.S.               <br /><br /><br />
Dollars (US$250,000) for each Calendar Year from the first year (1st) to the third year (3rd) of the      <br /><br /><br />
production period; One Hundred and Seventy-five Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$175,000) for each               <br /><br /><br />
Calendar Year from the fourth year (4th) to the ninth year (9th) of the production period and One         <br /><br /><br />
Hundred Thousand U.S. Dollars (US$100,000) for each Calendar Year from the tenth year (10th) to           <br /><br /><br />
the twentieth year (20th) of the production period. The aforesaid administrative fee will be paid in      <br /><br /><br />
two equal installments on the first of June and first of December of each Calendar Year.                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
5.2.15    Damages and losses to the assets:                                                               <br /><br /><br />
All costs and expenses necessary for the repair, replacement or supplement of the assets                  <br /><br /><br />
resulting from damages or losses incurred by fire, flood, storm, theft or any other force majeure         <br /><br /><br />
causes, excluding the losses specified in Article 8.4 of the Contract which shall be borne by the         <br /><br /><br />
Operator alone.                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

Costs incurred for personnel training pursuant to Article 16 of the Contract and Annex IV-                <br /><br /><br />
Training of Chinese Personnel and Transfer of Technology.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

﻿ 5.2.17 Miscellaneous expenses:                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Any reasonable miscellaneous expenses needed for the Petroleum Operations excluded in the                        <br /><br /><br />
above items of expenses, such as bank charges, books, stationery and conference expenses as well as              <br /><br /><br />
other reasonable expenses.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
5.2.18 Overhead:                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Overhead refers to the indirect costs for the managerial and operational services provided by                    <br /><br /><br />
the Operator's superior management organizations for the Petroleum Operations, including                         <br /><br /><br />
management, administration, accounting, treasury, inter-company audit, tax, legal matters,                       <br /><br /><br />
procurement, employee relations, financing, the collection of economic data and costs for general                <br /><br /><br />
consultation on such planning, design, research and operational activities, etc. to the extent that these        <br /><br /><br />
are not chargeable under Article 5.1.4 of this Accounting Procedure. The overhead for the Pilot Test             <br /><br /><br />
Operations shall be calculated in accordance with the following tiers and based on the sum of the total          <br /><br /><br />
actual costs from Article 5.2.1 through Article 5.2.17 and Article 5.2.19 of this Accounting Procedure,          <br /><br /><br />
but not including CNPC's assistance charges under Article 5.2.14.3 of this Accounting Procedure.                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 Direct Costs for Pilot Test                                                           Percentage Rate           <br /><br /><br />
 (U.S. S/Year)                                                                (%)                                <br /><br /><br />
 First Tier:                        0 to 5,000,000                            5%                                 <br /><br /><br />
 Second Tier:                       5,000,001 to 15,000,000                   3%                                 <br /><br /><br />
 Third Tier:                        15,000,001 to 25,000,000                  2%                                 <br /><br /><br />
 Fourth Tier:                       Over 25,000,000                           1%                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
The overhead rates for the Development Operations shall be agreed upon by the Parties                            <br /><br /><br />
through discussions at the time when the development budget is being prepared. However, direct                   <br /><br /><br />
costs for development shall not include investments on special items of construction which shall                 <br /><br /><br />
include, but not be limited to, gas processing facilities, terminal loading and other facilities of which        <br /><br /><br />
the overhead rates shall be agreed upon through discussions between the Parties at the time when the             <br /><br /><br />
development budget is being made.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
When the first budget is prepared for the Calendar Year of commencement of commercial                            <br /><br /><br />
production from the Oil Field, the overhead rates for production period and its related calculation              <br /><br /><br />
method as well as the utilization method shall be agreed upon through discussions between the                    <br /><br /><br />
Parties.                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
On the last working day of each month, the Operator shall make provision into the Joint                          <br /><br /><br />
Account for the overhead fees for the current month, calculated on the basis of cumulative actual                <br /><br /><br />
expenditure for the Calendar Year to that date and payment shall be made from the Joint Account on               <br /><br /><br />
the last working day of the following month. The final adjustment of the overhead shall be made at               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                        81                                                       <br /><br /><br />
﻿the end of the Calendar Year in respect to any difference between the actual payment by the Joint          <br /><br /><br />
Account and the total overhead for that Calendar Year calculated on the annual cumulative actual           <br /><br /><br />
investment expenditure at the end of such year. Any excess shall be refunded and deficiencies made         <br /><br /><br />
good.                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
5.2.19 General and administrative expenses:                                                                <br /><br /><br />
General and administrative expenses refer to the administrative expenses incurred for the                  <br /><br /><br />
offices established by the Operator within the Chinese territory and for JMC and its subordinate           <br /><br /><br />
bodies for the performance of the Petroleum Operations not otherwise directly chargeable pursuant to       <br /><br /><br />
Article 5.2 of the Accounting Procedure in accordance with the provisions of the Contract. Such            <br /><br /><br />
expenses shall be classified according to minor accounts.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
5.3    Except as otherwise provided in this Accounting Procedure, the allocation of common                 <br /><br /><br />
costs and expenses for each item of operations shall be provided by the Contractor if they are the Pilot   <br /><br /><br />
Test Costs and Development Costs and shall be charged in proportion to the Operating Costs actually        <br /><br /><br />
incurred in each month if they are the Operating Costs.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
5.4    With respect to the expenditures or excess expenditures as mentioned in Article                     <br /><br /><br />
10.2.4 (b) of the Contract which are determined by JMC to be unreasonable, JMC will form a joint           <br /><br /><br />
team for further investigation to determine whether they shall be charged to the Joint Account or shall    <br /><br /><br />
be borne by the Operator alone before the year-end final closing of accounts.                              <br /><br /><br />

﻿                   Article 6 Recovery of Costs                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
6.1    In accordance with the provisions of Article 12.2 of the Contract, the Operating Costs of            <br /><br /><br />
the Oil Field shall be recovered from the production of the Oil Field. In accordance with the               <br /><br /><br />
provisions of Article 12.3 of the Contract, the Pilot Test Costs and the Development Costs incurred by      <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor and the Pre-development Costs incurred by CNPC shall be recovered from the                   <br /><br /><br />
production of the Oil Field.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
6.2    At the date of completing each lifting of Crude Oil, the Operator shall make separate                <br /><br /><br />
records into the Joint Account for the appropriate reimbursement of the Operating Costs in                  <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Article 12.2 of the Contract. Written notices shall be sent by the Operator to CNPC         <br /><br /><br />
and the Investing Parties at the same time.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
6.3    In accordance with the provisions of Article 19.1 of the Contract, the Operator shall                <br /><br /><br />
establish complete books for recording the volume and value of Crude Oil and/or Natural Gas,                <br /><br /><br />
precisely reflecting the production and the disposal of the Crude Oil and/or Natural Gas within the         <br /><br /><br />
Contract Term.                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
6.4    Crude Oil production in each Calendar Year for the Oil Field within the production                   <br /><br /><br />
period shall be accounted according to the allocation proportions specified in Article 13 of the            <br /><br /><br />
Contract and at the Crude Oil price determined pursuant to Article 14.3 of the Contract.                    <br /><br /><br />

submitted within thirty (30) days after the end of each month, quarterly reports within forty-five (45)     <br /><br /><br />
days after the end of each Calendar Quarter and annual reports within forty-five (45) days after the        <br /><br /><br />
end of each Calendar Year. Monthly, quarterly and annual reports shall be submitted in accordance           <br /><br /><br />
with requirements and formats specified in the Accounting System.                                           <br /><br /><br />
7.2 Any Investing Party to the Contract may require the Operator to allow its staff to have                 <br /><br /><br />
access to the Joint Account Accounting Records relating to the application of expenses in the               <br /><br /><br />
stipulated custody period, upon giving thirty (30) days notice but such access shall not unduly hinder      <br /><br /><br />
the Operator’s normal operations.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

﻿        Article 9 Transfer Procedure for the Joint Account                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
9.1    If, at the expiration of the pilot test period, the Contractor opts to enter into the                <br /><br /><br />
development period, or when the Oil Field within the Contract Area goes from development into               <br /><br /><br />
production, or when the Contractor terminates the Contract, an inventory and check of all properties        <br /><br /><br />
and accounts shall be conducted.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
If the Contract has entered into the development period or the production period, the Operator              <br /><br /><br />
(after taking an inventory of all properties taken by all Investing Parties) shall make a proposal to       <br /><br /><br />
JMC for its approval listing the remaining equipment and Materials needed for the Petroleum                 <br /><br /><br />
Operations for the following period and which shall be carried forward to the next period in book           <br /><br /><br />
values in the Joint Account. The Operator shall be responsible for the disposal of the equipment and        <br /><br /><br />
materials not needed for the Petroleum Operations, the gains or losses derived from such disposal           <br /><br /><br />
shall be allocated in accordance with the share of each Investing Party in proportion to the overall        <br /><br /><br />
investment amount of all Investing Parties and be adjusted against the original accounts.                   <br /><br /><br />
If the Contract terminates, the method of an inventory to all of the remaining equipment and                <br /><br /><br />
Materials shall be the same as mentioned above, and the gains and losses derived from such disposal         <br /><br /><br />
shall be adjusted against the accounts of the original Investing Party in accordance with the above         <br /><br /><br />
mentioned methods.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
9.2    In accordance with the provisions of Article 8.9 of the Contract, when CNPC                          <br /><br /><br />
becomes the Operator of the Oil Fields within the Contract Area, the former Operator shall transfer to      <br /><br /><br />
CNPC all the Accounting Records relating to the Joint Account.                                              <br /><br /><br />
9.3    Upon the termination of the Contract, the Operator shall transfer all the relevant                   <br /><br /><br />
vouchers, books and statements over to CNPC for custody.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
9.4    In conducting the transfer of the accounting books and inventory and check of all the                <br /><br /><br />
properties in accordance with the provisions of this Accounting Procedure, the implementation               <br /><br /><br />
procedure for the transfer and verification, the accounting files to be transferred and accounting          <br /><br /><br />
matters to be settled as well as other details shall be agreed upon through consultation in advance         <br /><br /><br />
between the Operator and CNPC. The transfer procedure shall be completed within the time period             <br /><br /><br />
agreed upon by the Parties.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />

 Article 1 General Provisions                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
1.1    This Annex is an integral part of the Contract. The definitions set forth in Article 1 of                 <br /><br /><br />
the Contract are applicable to this Annex. If the provisions in this Annex are in conflict with those in         <br /><br /><br />
the Contract, the provisions of the Contract shall prevail.                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.2    The provisions in this Annex with respect to personnel costs shall only be applicable                     <br /><br /><br />
to the following personnel:                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(1)    representatives of JMC appointed by CNPC referred to in Article 7.1.1 of the                              <br /><br /><br />
Contract;                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(2)    personnel of CNPC in the subordinate bodies of JMC referred to in Article 7.4 of the                      <br /><br /><br />
Contract;                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(3)    professional representatives assigned by CNPC to the Operator’s (Contractor's)                            <br /><br /><br />
organizations referred to in Article 7.5 of the Contract; and                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(4)    personnel furnished by CNPC to the Contractor for employment (not including                               <br /><br /><br />
personnel recruited by CNPC for the Contractor) referred to in Article 2 hereof.                                 <br /><br /><br />
1.3    Personnel costs referred to in this Annex shall include salaries and wages of                             <br /><br /><br />
personnel specified in Article 3 hereof and other expenses specified in Article 4 hereof.                        <br /><br /><br />
1.4    There is a table attached to this Annex, i.e. Table of Salary and Wage Standards of                       <br /><br /><br />
Chinese Personnel.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

﻿                   Article 2 Employment of Chinese Personnel                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
2.1    The Contractor shall employ the Chinese Personnel in accordance with Article 15.2                  <br /><br /><br />
of the Contract.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
2.1.1    When employing the Chinese Personnel, the Contractor shall submit to CNPC a                      <br /><br /><br />
personnel employment plan, which shall specify specialties, number of personnel necessary to be           <br /><br /><br />
employed, and such requirements as to technique, experience and education, etc. with respect to the       <br /><br /><br />
personnel to be employed.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
2.1.2    CNPC shall, within sixty (60) days from the date on which it receives the personnel              <br /><br /><br />
employment plan submitted by the Contractor, notify the Contractor in a written form of the               <br /><br /><br />
following:                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(1)    names and specialties of employee candidates which will be furnished by CNPC, as                   <br /><br /><br />
well as their health conditions, working experience and education; and                                    <br /><br /><br />
(2)    specialties and number of employee candidates to be recruited by CNPC for the                      <br /><br /><br />
Contractor and provided by the Chinese organizations other than CNPC, as well as recruitment              <br /><br /><br />
arrangements with respect thereto.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
2.1.3    The employee candidates furnished and recruited by CNPC for the Contractor shall                 <br /><br /><br />
be employed by the Contractor only when they have passed tests conducted by the Contractor or             <br /><br /><br />
become qualified after being trained by the Contractor. The Contractor shall notify CNPC in writing       <br /><br /><br />
of the name list of the employee candidates whom it has decided to employ and whom it has decided         <br /><br /><br />
not to employ promptly after the tests or training have been conducted. The Contractor shall explain      <br /><br /><br />
the reason to CNPC with respect to the employee candidates whom it has decided not to employ. If          <br /><br /><br />
the explanation given by the Contractor is reasonable, CNPC shall promptly furnish or recruit             <br /><br /><br />
additional employee candidates.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
2.2 The employment contract(s) shall be signed by the Parties for employment of                           <br /><br /><br />
personnel furnished by CNPC who have passed the tests conducted by the Contractor or become               <br /><br /><br />
qualified after being trained by the Contractor. The said employment contract(s) shall include            <br /><br /><br />
provisions with respect to employees, such as employment, dismissal, resignation, production and          <br /><br /><br />
working assignments, salaries or wages and other expenses, awards and penalties, working time and         <br /><br /><br />
vacations, labor insurance and welfare, labor protection and labor discipline, etc. In addition, the      <br /><br /><br />
Parties shall work out specific stipulations with regard to the term of the employment contract(s),       <br /><br /><br />
conditions of termination and modification of employment contract(s), responsibilities in the case of     <br /><br /><br />
violation of the contract, and rights and obligations of the Parties.                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                89                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿2.3 The Contractor shall notify CNPC in writing thirty (30) days before dismissing or   <br /><br /><br />
replacing any personnel furnished by CNPC and employed by the Contractor.               <br /><br /><br />

﻿                    Article 3 Salaries and Wages of Personnel                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
3.1    Salaries and wages of the personnel referred to in Article 1.2 hereof (hereinafter                   <br /><br /><br />
referred to as “CNPC Personnel”) shall be dealt with in accordance with the following provisions:           <br /><br /><br />
3.1.1    CNPC Personnel shall be divided into two parts, i.e. personnel of JMC and                          <br /><br /><br />
employees. Personnel of JMC shall fall into two categories and employees shall fall into four               <br /><br /><br />
categories. The salaries and wages of the personnel in each category shall be classified as three           <br /><br /><br />
levels. The levels of the personnel in each category shall be determined in accordance with the             <br /><br /><br />
number of years of working experience they have. Those who have less than three (3) years of                <br /><br /><br />
working experience shall be determined as Level One; those who have three (3) to ten (10) years of          <br /><br /><br />
working experience shall be determined as Level Two; and those who have more than ten (10) years            <br /><br /><br />
of working experience shall be determined as Level Three. The salary and wage standards with                <br /><br /><br />
respect to Levels One, Two and Three of each category of personnel are specified in the Table of            <br /><br /><br />
Salary and Wage Standards of Chinese Personnel.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
3.1.2    The salary and wage standards specified in the Table of Salary and Wage Standards                  <br /><br /><br />
of Chinese Personnel, which are expressed in 1997 U.S. Dollars shall be increased annually in the           <br /><br /><br />
same percentage as the average annual increase percentage in base salaries granted to Expatriate            <br /><br /><br />
Employee.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
3.1.3    The salary and wage standards of personnel at each level in each category specified in             <br /><br /><br />
the Table of Salary and Wage Standards of Chinese Personnel divided by twenty-one point five (21.5)         <br /><br /><br />
shall be the daily salary and wage standards of personnel at such level in such category.                   <br /><br /><br />
3.2    Those CNPC Personnel who have worked for full eighteen (18) days shall be paid in                    <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the monthly salary and wage standards; those CNPC personnel who have worked for             <br /><br /><br />
less than full eighteen (18) days shall be paid in accordance with the daily salary and wage standards.     <br /><br /><br />
3.3    CNPC's chief representative of JMC shall always be paid in accordance with the                       <br /><br /><br />
salary and wage standards with respect to representatives of JMC. Other CNPC’s representatives of           <br /><br /><br />
JMC shall be paid, for the period in which he or she attends JMC meetings, in accordance with the           <br /><br /><br />
salary and wage standards with respect to representatives of JMC. If any professional representative        <br /><br /><br />
(including the secretary) of CNPC or any CNPC expert working in expert group(s) is concurrently a           <br /><br /><br />
representative of JMC (other than CNPC's chief representative of JMC), then he or she shall be paid,        <br /><br /><br />
for the period in which he or she attends JMC meetings, in accordance with the salary and wage              <br /><br /><br />
standards with respect to representatives of JMC, and for the rest of the period in accordance with the     <br /><br /><br />
salary and wage standards with respect to his or her actual post, i.e. the professional representatives     <br /><br /><br />
(including the secretary) shall be paid in accordance with the salary and wage standards with respect       <br /><br /><br />
to the professional representatives, and CNPC experts working in expert group(s) shall be paid in           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                               91                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿accordance with salary and wage standards with respect to the employees specified in the Table of        <br /><br /><br />
Salary and Wage Standards of Chinese Personnel.                                                          <br /><br /><br />
3.4    The initial determination and any subsequent modification with respect to any post                <br /><br /><br />
and level of representatives of JMC appointed by CNPC, secretaries, experts and professional             <br /><br /><br />
representatives of CNPC shall be made by CNPC in accordance with the number of years of working          <br /><br /><br />
experience and capabilities they have.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
The levels of the personnel furnished by CNPC and employed by the Contractor shall be                    <br /><br /><br />
determined in accordance with Article 3.1.1 herein, the posts of such personnel shall be determined by   <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor on the basis of assessment, and the subsequent promotion and demotion with respect to     <br /><br /><br />
the posts or levels of such personnel shall be determined by the Contractor. The aforesaid personnel     <br /><br /><br />
shall be paid in accordance with the salary and wage standards corresponding to their new posts from     <br /><br /><br />
the month following the month in which their posts or levels are promoted or demoted.                    <br /><br /><br />
3.5    The working time of the secretary, professional representatives and experts assigned              <br /><br /><br />
by CNPC to the subordinate bodies of JMC shall be determined in accordance with the working              <br /><br /><br />
system of JMC. However, the professional representatives of CNPC shall work for no more than five        <br /><br /><br />
(5) days per week and eight (8) hours per day.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

﻿                            Article 4 Other Expenses                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
4.1    CNPC Personnel shall be paid, in addition to the salaries and wages as stipulated in                <br /><br /><br />
Article 3 hereof, the following expenses.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
4.1.1    Expenses for working meals and transportation are as follows:                                     <br /><br /><br />
Four Hundred and Thirty (430) U.S. Dollars each month for each CNPC Personnel, of which:                   <br /><br /><br />
(1)    Ten (10) U.S. Dollars per day for each CNPC Personnel for working meals, Two                        <br /><br /><br />
Hundred and Fifteen (215) U.S. Dollars for each month;                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(2)    Ten (10) U.S. Dollars per day for each CNPC Personnel for transportation, Two                       <br /><br /><br />
Hundred and Fifteen (215) U.S. Dollars for each month.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
Those CNPC Personnel who have worked for eighteen (18) days in a month shall be paid in                    <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the monthly expenses for working meals and transportation; those CNPC Personnel            <br /><br /><br />
who have worked for less than eighteen (18) days in a month shall be paid in accordance with the           <br /><br /><br />
daily expenses for working meals and transportation.                                                       <br /><br /><br />
4.1.2    Allowance                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Any CNPC Personnel, who work on operating sites or on supporting base in desert, Gobi and                  <br /><br /><br />
offshore areas for performance of the Contract, shall obtain an allowance from thirty percent (30%) to     <br /><br /><br />
fifty percent (50%) of the daily salary or wage standards as stipulated in Article 3.1.3 hereof.           <br /><br /><br />
4.1.3    Expenses for visiting family:                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
4.1.3.1    Any CNPC Personnel whose cumulative working time in a Calendar Year reaches six                 <br /><br /><br />
(6) calendar months or more may enjoy a thirty (30) calendar day home leave with pay.                      <br /><br /><br />
4.1.3.2    Standards of home leave expenses for CNPC Personnel:                                            <br /><br /><br />
Three Hundred and Fifty (350) U.S. Dollars for each CNPC Personnel each time.                              <br /><br /><br />
The home leave frequency and the standards of expenses for any CNPC Personnel who work                     <br /><br /><br />
in remote area, desert, Gobi or offshore areas for the purpose of performance of the Contract shall be     <br /><br /><br />
decided through consultation between the Parties in view of the actual conditions.                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                              93                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿4.1.4 Premiums for accidental personal injury and death insurance and the expenses                        <br /><br /><br />
incurred in dealing with injuries or death of CNPC Personnel, which shall include:                        <br /><br /><br />
(a) Premiums for accidental personal injury and death insurance calculated in accordance                  <br /><br /><br />
with insured amount and insurance premium rate with respect to CNPC Personnel in each category;           <br /><br /><br />
and                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(b) Expenses actually incurred in dealing with injuries or death in the event that                        <br /><br /><br />
accidental injuries to or death of CNPC Personnel occur.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
4.1.5    Expenses for CNPC Personnel on business trips.                                                   <br /><br /><br />
4.1.6    Lodging expenses for CNPC Personnel working in the Petroleum operating area or                   <br /><br /><br />
the area where the JMC will locate for the purpose of performance of the Petroleum Operations if they     <br /><br /><br />
are not local residents there.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
4.2 In the event that commodity prices or transportation fees increase, the standards of                  <br /><br /><br />
expenses referred to in Articles 4.1.1, 4.1.2 and 4.1.3.2 herein shall be adjusted accordingly through    <br /><br /><br />
consultation by the Parties.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />

 Article I Use of Appropriate and Advanced Technology                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
Subject to the Contract, the Contractor agrees, in the implementation of Petroleum Operations,               <br /><br /><br />
to apply its appropriate and advanced technology and managerial experience including proprietary             <br /><br /><br />
technology, e.g. patented technology, know-how or other confidential technology, etc., and according         <br /><br /><br />
to the requirement of the progress of Petroleum Operations, the parties shall have scientific and            <br /><br /><br />
technical cooperation and academic exchange of views. The Contractor shall, at the request of JMC            <br /><br /><br />
according to the requirements of the Pilot Test Operations, Development Operations and Production            <br /><br /><br />
Operations, propose in advance the aforesaid specific items and submit them to JMC for discussion            <br /><br /><br />
and review.                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                  Article 2                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
            Objectives and Requirements of Training and Transfer of Technology                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
In accordance with Article 16 of the Contract, the Contractor shall train the Chinese                         <br /><br /><br />
Personnel, transfer its technology and managerial experience to CNPC and its Affiliates so as to              <br /><br /><br />
enable the Chinese Personnel to learn the use of the appropriate and advanced technology and                  <br /><br /><br />
managerial experience including proprietary technology, e.g. patented technology, etc. and to master          <br /><br /><br />
the knowledge and skill in the course of Petroleum Operations according to an agreed program, and to          <br /><br /><br />
obtain all the information and/or data needed for the performance of the Petroleum Operations, to             <br /><br /><br />
develop a competent, matured and well-trained Chinese Petroleum team. In the course of such                   <br /><br /><br />
training and transfer of technology, any proprietary technology and/or information including                  <br /><br /><br />
systematized technical data, information, software, specifications, manuals, operating procedure, etc.,       <br /><br /><br />
of the Contractor or its Affiliates, which are required in the Petroleum Operations hereunder, and            <br /><br /><br />
which involve royalty, may be used by CNPC and its Affiliates without royalty. However, CNPC                  <br /><br /><br />
shall not disclose any proprietary technology and/or information to any Third Party without the               <br /><br /><br />
written consent of the Contractor.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />

﻿ Article 3    Program of Training and Transfer of Technology                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
3.1    Respectively before the commencement of the Pilot Test Operations, Development                       <br /><br /><br />
Operations and Production Operations, the Contractor shall, in advance, consult with the                    <br /><br /><br />
representatives of CNPC in JMC and prepare a draft program of personnel training and transfer of            <br /><br /><br />
technology and managerial experience respectively for the aforesaid three periods and submit them to        <br /><br /><br />
JMC for discussion and approval. After approval by JMC, the Contractor shall put them into practice.        <br /><br /><br />
3.2    In accordance with the aforesaid program approved by JMC and actual requirement of                   <br /><br /><br />
the Petroleum Operations, the Contractor shall work out a plan for each year respectively during pilot      <br /><br /><br />
test, development and production periods. After such plan is approved by JMC, in accordance with the        <br /><br /><br />
provisions of Article 7.2.10 and Article 10 of the Contract, it shall become an integral part of the        <br /><br /><br />
Contractor's annual Work Program and the Contractor shall be responsible for its implementation,            <br /><br /><br />
including trainee study inspection, test and certification.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
3.3    The program and plan submitted by the Contractor for the training of the Chinese                     <br /><br /><br />
Personnel and transfer of technology shall include at least the fields of specialization, specialized       <br /><br /><br />
technology, scope of personnel, specific job categories, type, method, the number of personnel, timing,     <br /><br /><br />
location, budget and objective to be reached, as well as the method of inspection of the trainee's          <br /><br /><br />
progress, examination, and certification of course completion.                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                  99                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿                        Article 4 Scope of Training and Transfer of Technology                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
4.1    Subject to the Contract, the Parties agree that the Contractor shall, according to the                                            <br /><br /><br />
requirements of the Petroleum Operations under the Contract, train the Chinese Personnel and transfer                                    <br /><br /><br />
its technology and managerial experience to CNPC, including, but not limited to, the following fields                                    <br /><br /><br />
of specialization:                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
A.    Petroleum geology, geochemistry, geophysical data collection, conventional and                                                     <br /><br /><br />
special processing and interpretation, well logging data, conventional and special processing and                                        <br /><br /><br />
interpretation, well testing and the evaluation of oil and gas resources;                                                                <br /><br /><br />
B.    Development geology, digital simulation and physical modeling of Oil Field                                                         <br /><br /><br />
development, development seismic data collection, conventional and special processing and                                                <br /><br /><br />
interpretation, reservoir and development engineering, feasibility study and evaluation of Oil Field                                     <br /><br /><br />
development, formulation of the Overall Development Program, the evaluation of early production or                                       <br /><br /><br />
appraisal trial production;                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
C.    Environmental conditions for construction, engineering project management,                                                         <br /><br /><br />
engineering planning, design, construction and installation, pipeline laying technique, oil and gas                                      <br /><br /><br />
gathering and processing, transportation of Crude Oil;                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
D.    Oil and/or gas recovery technology including production automation, remote sensing                                                 <br /><br /><br />
and control, and technology of secondary and tertiary recovery;                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
E.    Directional drilling procedures, optimum drilling, formation pore pressure estimation                                              <br /><br /><br />
and blowout control;                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
F.    Economic evaluation, finance and control, procurement, sales, development of                                                       <br /><br /><br />
personnel ability and contract administration;                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
G.    Laws, safety, fire fighting and lifesaving, environmental protection, communications                                               <br /><br /><br />
and other fields of specialization related to the Contract.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
4.2    The Parties agree that during the pilot test period the Contractor shall, in accordance                                           <br /><br /><br />
with the fields of specialization specified in Article 4.1 herein, transfer systematically and in complete                               <br /><br /><br />
sets to CNPC the Contractor's specialized technology and managerial experience, which include, but                                       <br /><br /><br />
are not limited to the following:                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
A. Pumping recovery,                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                     100                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
﻿B.    Secondary and tertiary recovery; and                                                              <br /><br /><br />
C.    Petrology and physical properties of reservoir rocks.                                             <br /><br /><br />
During the development period and production period, the specialized technology and                     <br /><br /><br />
managerial experience transferred to CNPC from the Contractor shall be proposed by the Contractor       <br /><br /><br />
prior to the approval of the Overall Development Program of the Oil Field and the commencement of       <br /><br /><br />
commercial production therefrom respectively, and be included in the phase plan after a decision is     <br /><br /><br />
made thereupon by the Parties through consultation.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
4.3 Subject to the Contract, the Parties agree that the Contractor shall train Chinese                  <br /><br /><br />
Personnel, transfer technology and teach managerial knowledge to CNPC including, but not limited to,    <br /><br /><br />
the following personnel areas:                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
4.3.1    The Contractor shall transfer its technology to the Chinese Personnel who have been            <br /><br /><br />
assigned to work in subordinate bodies of JMC and teach them managerial experience.                     <br /><br /><br />
4.3.2    The Contractor shall train the Chinese Personnel who have been assigned to the                 <br /><br /><br />
Contractor including the Chinese Personnel who have been employed by the Contractor for the             <br /><br /><br />
performance of the Contract and transfer technology to them in order to improve their technical and/or  <br /><br /><br />
managerial capabilities.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
4.3.3    The Contractor shall in advance train the Chinese Personnel who will be employed by            <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor for development and production of the Oil Fields.                                        <br /><br /><br />
4.3.4    The Contractor shall train the Chinese Personnel who work in the departments of                <br /><br /><br />
CNPC which are directly related to, or provide directly various services for the performance of the     <br /><br /><br />
Contract, and transfer technology to them.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
4.4    Within the fields of specialization specified in Articles 4.1 and 4.2 herein, as required        <br /><br /><br />
for the performance of the Petroleum Operations under the Contract, the Chinese Personnel referred to   <br /><br /><br />
in Article 4.3 may include, but shall not be limited to, the following specific job categories;         <br /><br /><br />
A.    Geologists, geophysicists, geochemists, petroleum engineers, paleontologists, seismic             <br /><br /><br />
data collection and conventional and special processing and interpretation engineers, well logging data <br /><br /><br />
conventional and special processing and interpretation engineers;                                       <br /><br /><br />
B.    Development geologists, reservoir and development engineers, experts for digital                  <br /><br /><br />
simulation and physical modeling of the Oil Field development, engineers for development seismic        <br /><br /><br />
data collection, conventional and special processing and interpretation engineers, formulation of       <br /><br /><br />
Overall Development Program engineers;                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿C. Experts for engineering geology, engineering construction managers and supervisors,                         <br /><br /><br />
engineering design, construction and installation engineers, pipeline laying engineers, oil and/or gas         <br /><br /><br />
gathering and processing engineers;                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
D. Production engineers, automation engineers, remote sensing and control engineers,                           <br /><br /><br />
secondary and tertiary recovery, production and maintenance personnel and supervisors;                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 E. Drilling engineers, mud engineers, drilling managers and supervisors;                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
F. Petroleum economists, accountants, auditors, finance managers, planning managers,                           <br /><br /><br />
procurement managers, oil and gas sales managers;                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 G. Computer hardware engineers, computer software engineers, laboratory engineers and                         <br /><br /><br />
operators, communication engineers, safety engineers, pollution prevention engineers, experts working          <br /><br /><br />
in business transactions, material and warehouse engineers;                                                    <br /><br /><br />
All the training or employment candidates for the aforesaid job categories shall be selected in                <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the requirements of various periods of the Petroleum Operations under the Contract             <br /><br /><br />
The Contractor shall propose the criteria for the selection, and CNPC shall, pursuant to such criteria,        <br /><br /><br />
provide a list of candidates. If such candidates are not able to meet the requirements of the Contractor,      <br /><br /><br />
CNPC shall provide additional candidates. The Parties shall discuss and decide who will finally be             <br /><br /><br />
selected.                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

﻿             Article 5 Type of Training and Transfer of Technology                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
5.1    The Contractor agrees to train Chinese Personnel in various and efficient ways and to              <br /><br /><br />
transfer its technology and managerial experience to CNPC to the extent reasonably possible pursuant      <br /><br /><br />
to a program agreed by JMC, including but not limited to the following:                                   <br /><br /><br />
5.1.1    With the consent of JMC, the Contractor shall provide necessary training equipment               <br /><br /><br />
and training materials so as to give the Chinese Personnel the technology, management and language        <br /><br /><br />
training, and all the expenditures hereunder shall be within the spending limitation for training of      <br /><br /><br />
Chinese Personnel. When necessary, the Contractor shall send its experts to the People’s Republic of      <br /><br /><br />
China to give special training courses.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
5.1.2    The Contractor shall send the Chinese Personnel to study in training centers, training           <br /><br /><br />
schools and institutes inside or outside the People's Republic of China, as well as in some special       <br /><br /><br />
scientific research institutes, computer centers, and engineering design companies. Some of them          <br /><br /><br />
shall have the opportunity to be able to obtain certain technical qualifications or academic degrees.     <br /><br /><br />
5. 1. 3 The training and the transfer of technology and managerial experience shall be                    <br /><br /><br />
realized through working together with Contractor's experts in offices and on operating sites of the      <br /><br /><br />
Contractor inside or outside the People's Republic of China.                                              <br /><br /><br />
5.1. 4 The Contractor shall endeavor to persuade the Subcontractors to train the Chinese                  <br /><br /><br />
Personnel and transfer technology to them.                                                                <br /><br /><br />
5.1.5 With respect to any specialized technology and managerial experience to be                          <br /><br /><br />
transferred by the Contractor to CNPC, the Parties shall organize special personnel to be responsible     <br /><br /><br />
for its execution and realization in accordance with the schedule.                                        <br /><br /><br />

﻿            Article 6 Scientific and Technical Cooperation and Exchange                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
6.1    The Parties agree, in accordance with the requirements of Petroleum Operations                         <br /><br /><br />
under the Contract, to have scientific and technical cooperation and academic exchange of views,              <br /><br /><br />
within the fields of specialization specified in Article 4.1 of this Annex. The Parties shall discuss and     <br /><br /><br />
propose a plan, items, personnel and type of scientific and technical cooperation and academic                <br /><br /><br />
exchange of views for each year in a phased manner, and submit them to JMC for discussion and                 <br /><br /><br />
approval. After approval by JMC, the Contractor shall incorporate them in the phased plans and put            <br /><br /><br />
them into practice.                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
6.2    The personnel participating in the scientific and technical cooperation and academic                   <br /><br /><br />
exchange of views shall be experts, engineers and technicians from scientific research and designing          <br /><br /><br />
departments related to the Contract. The Parties shall provide them with necessary facilities and             <br /><br /><br />
assistance for scientific researches, as required to carry out any plan approved by the JMC for               <br /><br /><br />
scientific and technical cooperation.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
6.3    The Contractor shall furnish CNPC worldwide information concerning Petroleum                           <br /><br /><br />
science and technology, economics, legal and managerial topics. According to the requirement of               <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations, scientific and technical seminars shall be jointly held by the Parties through          <br /><br /><br />
consultation. The Contractor shall invite the Chinese Personnel to attend relevant scientific and             <br /><br /><br />
technical seminars organized solely by the Contractor or jointly with others and shall assist the             <br /><br /><br />
Chinese Personnel to get permits to attend international conferences relating to Petroleum technology,        <br /><br /><br />
economics and legal topics and to participate in other relevant activities.                                   <br /><br /><br />

﻿                        Article 2 Ownership of the Data                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
2.1    The ownership of all of the data, records, vouchers and other original data obtained                <br /><br /><br />
and/or acquired by the Contractor in the implementation of the Contract shall vest in CNPC.                <br /><br /><br />
2.2    The ownership and right of use of cores, rock samples, oil samples and other samples                <br /><br /><br />
obtained and/or acquired by the Contractor from the Contract Area shall vest in CNPC.                      <br /><br /><br />
2.3    Within the validity period of the Contract, after the termination of the Contract and               <br /><br /><br />
after the Contractor assigns its rights and obligations, no data, information and samples mentioned in     <br /><br /><br />
Articles 2.1 and 2.2 hereof shall be disclosed in any way to a Third Party except as stipulated in         <br /><br /><br />
Articles 3.4 and 3.5 hereof or be transferred, donated, exchanged, sold, or published in any form          <br /><br /><br />
without the permission in writing of CNPC.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
