                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                             108                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿ Article 3                                       Control and Use of the Data                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
3.1    During the implementation of the Petroleum Operations, the Contractor shall be                         <br /><br /><br />
responsible to keep in good order, all the data, information and samples stipulated in Articles 2.1 and       <br /><br /><br />
2.2 hereof within the territory of the People's Republic of China and shall furnish CNPC in a timely          <br /><br /><br />
manner with such data, information and samples for use and turn them over to CNPC in a step-by-step           <br /><br /><br />
or phase-by-phase manner.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
3.2    The Contractor shall have the right to use or duplicate the data and information                       <br /><br /><br />
mentioned in Article 2.1 hereof and use samples referred to in Article 2.2 hereof within and outside          <br /><br /><br />
China and the results of research, interpretation, analysis and chemical examination shall be submitted       <br /><br /><br />
or reported to CNPC in a timely manner. The Contractor shall not use the above-mentioned data,                <br /><br /><br />
information and samples for purposes other than those related to the implementation of the Contract.          <br /><br /><br />
3.3    Any shipment abroad for use of the original data and information (such as original                     <br /><br /><br />
magnetic tapes, original recordings, etc.) referred to in Article 2.1 hereof and of the samples referred      <br /><br /><br />
to in Article 2.2 hereof shall be subject to the consent in writing of CNPC. Unless otherwise agreed by       <br /><br /><br />
CNPC, the size of any piece of core or amount of any batch of rock cuttings and samples to be                 <br /><br /><br />
shipped abroad shall not be greater than one half (1/2) of the total size or amount of the original piece     <br /><br /><br />
or batch. The original data and information shipped abroad shall, upon completion of the use or               <br /><br /><br />
duplication thereof, be shipped in a timely manner back to and be kept in China.                              <br /><br /><br />
3.4    If, for the purpose of implementation of the Contract, the Contractor needs to provide                 <br /><br /><br />
the data and information for such Third Parties as banks or other credit institutions, Subcontractors         <br /><br /><br />
and potential assignees to which the rights and interests under the Contract are assigned, the type and       <br /><br /><br />
scope of the data and information to be provided shall be subject to consent by CNPC and the                  <br /><br /><br />
Contractor shall obtain from such Third Parties a written undertaking that they shall have the                <br /><br /><br />
obligation to keep the provided data and information confidential.                                            <br /><br /><br />
3.5    The Contractor may provide such data and information as may be requested by their                      <br /><br /><br />
parent corporations or Affiliates relating to the implementation of the Contract or by securities and         <br /><br /><br />
exchange organizations or the governments of the Contractor’s home countries, subject to the prior            <br /><br /><br />
reporting thereof to CNPC. The Contractor shall inform the aforesaid parent corporations or                   <br /><br /><br />
Affiliates which receive the data and information that they shall be obligated to keep such data and          <br /><br /><br />
information confidential and shall request the security and exchange organizations or the governments         <br /><br /><br />
of their home countries to keep such data and information confidential subject to international               <br /><br /><br />
practice.                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
3.6    Release of the data and information to the press shall be subject to the consultation                  <br /><br /><br />
and agreement between the Parties.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿               Article 4 Scope of the Data Provided for CNPC                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
In carrying out the Petroleum Operations, the Contractor shall provide CNPC with data and              <br /><br /><br />
information, including, but not limited to the following:                                              <br /><br /><br />
4.1    Overall programs and plans of operations and information and documents of designs               <br /><br /><br />
of an individual project:                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
4.1.1    Pilot test program of the Contract Area;                                                      <br /><br /><br />
4.1.2    Annual operational plans for pilot test;                                                      <br /><br /><br />
4.1.3    Pilot test program;                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
4.1.4    Designs for sidetrack, well repair, well recompletion and single well injectivity test        <br /><br /><br />
and designs for single well new technique test and well groups displacement tests for the purpose of   <br /><br /><br />
pilot test;                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
4.1.5    Early development programs, overall development programs and adjusted                         <br /><br /><br />
development programs of Oil Fields;                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
4.1.6    Plans for production and production testing of wells and Oil Fields;                          <br /><br /><br />
4.1.7    The content and general schedules of engineering projects;                                    <br /><br /><br />
4.1.8    Basic designs of engineering projects (e.g. oil, gas and water treatment facility,            <br /><br /><br />
modules and pipelines);                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
4.1.9    Annual and monthly operational progress charts for engineering projects;                      <br /><br /><br />
4.1.10    Procurement plans and schedules for engineering projects;                                    <br /><br /><br />
4.1.11    Test-run and commissioning schedules for engineering projects.                               <br /><br /><br />
4.2 Information and documents on the progress of all operations:                                       <br /><br /><br />
4.2.1 Daily, monthly and annual reports on well drilling and production testing;                       <br /><br /><br />

4.3.7    All the samples (including cores, cuttings, oil, gas and water samples and mud                <br /><br /><br />
